# Atlas Wiki Index

Authoritative accumulated-context source for the OGDEN Atlas project.
Read this first at the start of every session.

## Orientation
- [SCHEMA.md](SCHEMA.md) — Wiki conventions and page templates
- [log.md](log.md) — Chronological operation log
- [LAUNCH-CHECKLIST.md](LAUNCH-CHECKLIST.md) — Pre-commercial blockers (legal, ops, compliance)

## Entities
- [Atlas Platform](entities/atlas-platform.md) — Project overview, stack, completion status, launch blockers
- [API Backend](entities/api.md) — Fastify routes, patterns, services, dependencies
- [Web App](entities/web-app.md) — React SPA, dashboard groups, Zustand stores, feature structure
- [Shared Package](entities/shared-package.md) — Zod schemas, utilities, constants
- [Database](entities/database.md) — PostgreSQL/PostGIS schema (12 tables), connection pattern
- [Data Pipeline](entities/data-pipeline.md) — BullMQ orchestration, layer adapters, workers
- [PDF Export Service](entities/pdf-export-service.md) — Puppeteer templates, S3 storage, 7 export types
- [Gap Analysis](entities/gap-analysis.md) — ~120 gaps against global frameworks (FAO, USDA, ASTM, IUCN), triage roadmap
- [Showcase Portal](entities/showcase-portal.md) — Public scrollytelling portal at `/showcase/three-streams` + 3 tier sub-routes; cold-visitor Y0→Y2 narrative on static SSG (Phase 3, shipped 2026-05-21)
- [Site Annotations Store](entities/site-annotations-store.md) — Persisted store for user-authored OBSERVE annotations (hazards, transects, sectors, ecology, succession, SWOT)
- [PlacedFeaturesCard](entities/placed-features-card.md) — Right-rail inventory of every feature placed on the map, unified across three stores (built / design / zone) and scoped per stage (observe / plan)
- [Act Tier Shell](entities/act-tier-shell.md) — Default map-centric Act page; objective-driven categorized tools rail (`objectiveActTools` map + `actToolCatalog`) arming real placements through Act/Observe/Plan DrawHosts on one canvas (ADR-7 add-only seam)
- [Plan Tier Shell](entities/plan-tier-shell.md) — Default map-centric Plan page; mirrors Act's 4-rail tier shell 1:1 (`PlanTierShell` + `planToolCatalog` + `PlanTierCategorizedToolsRail`) but with an **editable** center design canvas and the Plan **locking** status engines, plus a Plan-only `'modules'` tool category opening `PlanModuleSlideUp`. Promoted to default for every project via `getPlanShellMode` (legacy `stratum-spine`/`module-bar` preserved + toggle-reachable, commit `56b8170b`)
- [Closed-loop Workflow](entities/closed-loop-workflow.md) — Multi-session epic realizing the `olos-waste-vector-v2.jsx` prototype as a Plan→Approval→Act closed-loop / waste-vector workflow (Plan-side enrichment of `closedLoopStore`/`WasteVectorTool`; Act half over the dormant `stewardshipRoutineStore`). Shared `MaterialFlow` design-intent contract (operationalStatus/cadence/via-nodes/activeMonths + config maps) + pure `flowStatusModel`. Slice A0 shipped 2026-06-03
- [Protocols Dashboard](entities/protocols-dashboard.md) — Fourth peer surface (`/v3/project/$projectId/protocols`) alongside Observe/Plan/Act; first OLOS Protocol-System vertical slice (evolve-in-place). Widens the model with four **severity tiers** (`SeverityTier` + literal-hex/glyph `TIER_VISUAL`: Stop `✕`/Respond `▲`/Watch `●`/Abundance `♥`) + an immutable `ProtocolActivation` (frozen `recipeSnapshot`); `protocolStore` gains an `activations` slice (persist v2). Active view = `TierBadge` per active template + a recent-activations strip; RESPOND wired end to end via a Trigger Recognition bottom sheet on Act proof capture. Nav via a thin `ProjectBundleBar` link (spine doesn't enumerate Protocols)
- [Observe Dashboard](entities/observe-dashboard.md) — Read-only synthesis layer; 4 surfaces (Unified land state / Domain Detail / Temporal / Objective rollup) branched by a route-derived `surface` discriminator. Domain Detail carries an `All / From Act / Baseline` source filter; Surface 4 rolls observations up per Plan objective via `sourceObjectiveId`, and each rollup card deep-links into its primary-domain Domain Detail pre-filtered to "From Act" via a typed `?source=` search param (`7ecf69f3`)
- [Three Streams Farm](entities/three-streams-farm.md) — Fictional Ontario showcase farm canon (rural Milton, ~180 acres, 8-year arc)
- [Ecosystem Farm Template](entities/ecosystem-farm-template.md) — Public, system-owned project template extracted from Three Streams canon; per-tier ContactCTA deep links instantiate against visitor boundary (Phase 4, shipped 2026-05-21)
- [Organization](entities/organization.md) — Multi-tenant workspace primitive: register-time auto-org for all tiers, `projects.org_id NOT NULL` invariant, Stewarding-tier `/organizations/new` prelude with progressive disclosure (Phase 4.5, shipped 2026-05-21)

## Concepts
- [Design System](concepts/design-system.md) — cool-grey chrome + estate gold/sage (earth ramp → `--color-neutral-*`, warm hues reserved for map data, 2026-05-25), Fira Code/Sans, component tokens
- [Scoring Engine](concepts/scoring-engine.md) — 8 weighted dimensions + 2-3 classifications, ~140+ components, WithConfidence, Tier 3 integration
- [Financial Model](concepts/financial-model.md) — Cost/revenue/cashflow engine, CostRange, mission scoring
- [Local-First Architecture](concepts/local-first-architecture.md) — Zustand + localStorage (~70 `ogden-` stores); `syncService` is wired but **partial** — only 4 slices (projects/zones/structures/comments) sync, the rest is localStorage-only; project-bundle is the multi-device escape hatch (corrected 2026-05-16). Project create is now single-pathed + idempotent via `syncProjectNow` (2026-05-31, [[decisions/2026-05-31-atlas-project-sync-hardening]]); the server-only `parcelBoundaryGeojson:null` centroid gap is CLOSED via `hydrateProjectBoundaries` (2026-06-01, commit `5aa973a4`, [[log/2026-06-01-atlas-boundary-hydration-gap-closed]]) — type-clean but not yet live-screenshot-verified
- [External Data Sources — Phase 8 Reference](concepts/external-data-sources.md) — Attribution, licence, refresh-cadence, and verification-checklist for the deferred-Phase-8 datasets (WorldCover, NLCD, ACI, Theobald HM, IGRAC, WDPA, NCED, ECCC ESG); flags the unresolved IGRAC CC-BY vs CC-BY-NC contradiction in the source ADR
- [Feature Manifest](concepts/feature-manifest.md) — 30-section source-of-truth for features, phase gating, scaffolding generator
- [Permaculture Alignment](concepts/permaculture-alignment.md) — 3 ethics + 12 Holmgren principles assessment from 2026-04-28 Permaculture Scholar dialogue; 4 represented / 6 partial / 3 missing; six prioritised recommendations
- [OLOS Story → Codebase Map](concepts/olos-story-codebase-map.md) — the 17-chapter OLOS narrative's 12 depicted capabilities cross-referenced to shipped code (verified 2026-05-23); 7 Full / 5 Partial / 0 Missing; the alignment review's two P0s (needs-&-yields, temporal slider) have shipped
- [Atlas Sidebar — Permaculture-Grounded IA](concepts/atlas-sidebar-permaculture.md) — **[DEPRECATED for forward IA, superseded 2026-05-16](decisions/2026-05-16-atlas-7-stage-lifecycle-retirement.md)]** 2026-04-28 Permaculture Scholar synthesis on lifecycle sidebar IA; 4 of 7 verbs renamed (Observe/Test/Steward/Evaluate), Steward-as-loop, 4 utility nav items prioritised — rationale retained as history, recommendations superseded by the 7-stage-retirement ADR
- [Module-page template (Atlas-UI)](concepts/module-page-template.md) — Locked JSX + CSS contract for module home pages: `<TopStageBar>` + `module-frame` wrapper, no per-page topbar overrides; Stage 2 inherits the same shell
- [Backlog — Full `syncService` Coverage (2026-05-16)](concepts/full-syncservice-coverage-backlog.md) — Approved-but-deferred durable fix for P0-1 multi-device silent data loss: hybrid storage (typed tables for vegetation/succession + generic `project_state_blobs` for the rest, design elements stay on `design_features`), per-store `rev` stale-write reject + visible conflict, `syncManifest.ts` as CI-enforced single source of truth, phased shadow→typed→blob rollout. ~128k-token multi-session build; bundle hatch holds the testing window. Full plan in the approved plan file.
- [P2 Backlog — Pre-Live-Testing Hardening (2026-05-16)](concepts/p2-pre-testing-backlog.md) — 7 catalogued-not-executed P2 items from the pre-testing pass (manifest status drift, citation:null cost rows, caveats[] truncation, IGRAC licence contradiction, regenerationPlanStore stub-migrate hardening [corrected: it **is** UI-mounted], map-overlay chrome, SlideUpPanel/RailPanelShell focus-trap audit); none are testing-window blockers
- [Parallel Session Coordination](concepts/parallel-session-coordination.md) — Protocol for two Claude Code sessions concurrently force-pushing `feat/atlas-permaculture`: rebase rules, `--force-with-lease` only, per-day `wiki/log/YYYY-MM-DD-slug.md` files (no monolith collision), pre-push hook safety net. Triggered by the 2026-05-20 silently-dropped log entry.
- [Decision Groups](concepts/decision-groups.md) — Plan-layer editorial grouping of an objective's Act-layer checklist items (`decisionGroups[]`, Secondary Layer Spec v1.2 sections 9.3-9.4 + Decision Groups Reference v1.0). **Encoded end-to-end** (2026-05-31): schema + resolver + Plan render + all catalogues + tests. ADR [[decisions/2026-05-31-atlas-decision-groups-encode]].
- [Project Type Graduation](concepts/project-type-graduation.md) — Grow-into-types model: append-only `type_history[]`, derived `active_primary_types[]`, P1-P5 primary+primary tensions (Graduation Spec v1.0). **Planned, not yet encoded** (2026-05-30 wiki-ingest).
- [Land OS Positioning & Phase-2 Roadmap](concepts/land-os-positioning.md) — **Ratified Phase-2 north star.** Verbatim success definition (run an Apricot-Lane-complexity project without external PM tools), the 5-capability model + capability→current-state map (Observe/Plan/Phased = built engines; Manage = the big gap = Track D; Adapt = monitoring built + recommend-engine = D5), A/B/C/D sequencing (A complete, B track-level, C intent-only Scholar-gated, D decomposed), full Sub-project D **D0–D5** backlog with dependencies, and the load-bearing **C-vs-D covenant boundary** (D3/D5 are cost/budget tracking only; financing stays in C). Roadmap is capability/track-based, not 7-stage-lifecycle-based.

## Decisions
- [2026-06-11 Draw-time placement rules: shared catalog, client gate, server PostGIS guard](decisions/2026-06-11-atlas-placement-rules-architecture.md) -- Operator: drawing tools must enforce placement logic (zone placement, buffer/setback distances), tiered block/warn, client AND server. **One rule source, three consumers:** 14-entry data-only catalog in `@ogden/shared/placementRules` (6 block all `serverEnforceable` / 8 warn; `PLACEMENT_DISTANCES_M` single distance source -- `SETBACK_RULES` re-bases onto it so draw-time and post-hoc numbers can never diverge; `amanahNote` on 4 rules: huquq al-jar, tahara, water-source protection per the Prophet's ﷺ prohibition, khushuʿ); client turf evaluator (`apps/web/src/v3/plan/validation/` -- pre-buffered context never on mousemove, ALL MultiPolygon parts, zone rules no-op without zones, annotations exempt) + `PlacementConflictDialog` warn-acknowledgment (>=3 chars, persisted as `placementAcknowledgments`), wired into 14 dedicated tools + `useDesignElementDrawTool` (70+ kinds) before skeleton creation + drag-moves on mouseup; server PostGIS guard `placementGuard.ts` (`ST_Covers`/`ST_DWithin(geography)`/`ST_Intersects`, `PLACEMENT_GUARD_MODE=off|log|enforce` default `log`, 409 `PLACEMENT_VIOLATION`, transactional bulk rollback, syncService acks + sync-failed surfacing); RulesPanel consolidation via `placementRuleToCatalogEntry` (legacy-id dedup, `drawTime` badges, amanah notes rendered). Setback rings stay static -- enforcement reads live geometry (per the `setbackStore.ts` ADR). 10 mock-DB + 6 native-PG integration tests green (plan gate verbatim: well at 20 m -> 409, 40 m -> 201). **Notable find:** pre-existing PATCH jsonb double-encode corruption in design-features (postgres.js re-stringifies string params bound to jsonb placeholders) -- fixed via `db.json()`; rule on record: never bind a pre-stringified string to a jsonb placeholder. Deferred: auto-design post-stamp validation (plan 5.2); `Z_TO_CATEGORIES`/`zoneAffinity` deliberately NOT merged. Commits `0694ee1c`->`924d0254` on `main`, not pushed. Amanah: the rules *encode* covenant constraints (neighbour rights, purity, water protection, khushuʿ) -- no capital/sale/financing surface, no CSRA/salam ([[fiqh-csra-erased-2026-05-04]]). Entities [[entities/shared-package]], [[entities/api]], [[entities/web-app]]; Log [[log/2026-06-12-atlas-placement-rules-completion-audit]].
- [2026-06-11 Item-level completion-path audit + ratchet (in-app completability)](decisions/2026-06-11-atlas-completion-path-audit-ratchet.md) -- Operator: every stratum objective/checklist item must be completable inside OLOS without external tools, for an **ecovillage (intentional community) + orchards + food-forest guilds + silvopasture + nursery**; operator fork: **audit + ratchet first**, close gaps in priority order in later sessions. **Decision:** shared classifier `packages/shared/src/relationships/objectiveCompletionPaths.ts` with a DI'd `ActToolArmIndex` (shared cannot import the lucide-bearing app tool catalog -- same DI pattern as `actToolCoverage.test.ts`); per-item classifications `auto-answer | auto-formula | form-capture | objective-map | objective-log | objective-flow | no-path` (only `auto-*` + `form-capture` are per-item evidence-backed -- honesty note in header); app-layer 4-test ratchet (`completionPathAudit.ratchet.test.ts` + `completionPathGaps.baseline.json`: no new gaps, no stale entries, same pair for objective-spatial-only, unmatched form-arm `formId`s pinned); report emitter `scripts/audit-checklist-completion-paths.ts` with `--write-baseline` so fixture and report can never disagree. **Pinned: 2029 checklist items / 355 objectives; 610 no-path (30.1%); 232 evidence-backed (215 form + 13 formula + 4 answer); worst strata s7 (225), s4 (208), s6 (132).** Gap-closure priority: universal -> ev- -> orch- -> silv- -> nur- -> hms- -> others (the operator's actual composition). Framing: `Ecovillage (Intentional Community)` relabel (data-only, operator to confirm); spineGate conformance pins the ecovillage + orchard_food_forest + silvopasture + nursery combo; NO new project type (earlier unauthored-ecovillage claim was wrong). Commits `fa920b6c` + `d7df22cc` on `main`, not pushed. Amanah: audit/measurement tooling only -- no capital/sale/financing surface, no CSRA/salam ([[fiqh-csra-erased-2026-05-04]]); the no-path backlog includes financial-planning items whose future captures must be designed Amanah-clean ([[feedback-csa-in-catalogues]]). Entity [[entities/shared-package]]; Log [[log/2026-06-12-atlas-placement-rules-completion-audit]].
- [2026-06-11 Decision workbench moves from Act to Plan (Act becomes execution-only)](decisions/2026-06-11-atlas-workbench-act-to-plan.md) -- Operator: "transfer the decision making workspace often referred to as the 'workbench' from the Act stage to the Plan stage." Reverses the "Phase B" framing (decisions worked through in Act). The interactive `ActTierZeroWorkbench` (ACTIVE DECISION / WORKING-ON two-pane, "Record this decision") moves from `ActTierShell` to `PlanTierShell` via a center-canvas swap on the 25 `TIER_ZERO_OBJECTIVE_IDS`; Act's center becomes a full-width read-only `ActTierExecutionPanel` (`.tierZeroExec`). **3 steps:** (1) NEW shared `tierZeroObjectives.ts` (id set + `isTierZeroObjective`/`isTierZeroObjectiveId`, lifted out of `ActTierShell`); (2) `PlanTierShell` mounts `<ActTierZeroWorkbench>` (imported unchanged, [[feedback-no-deletion]]) with cold-hydration guard + tools-tray/`VisionFormsTabsModal` suppression, wired to `actEvidenceStore`; (3) Act drops the workbench + dead handlers, keeps `handleFormDataSave`. **Lock asymmetry now correct:** the workbench sits behind Plan's prerequisite locks (Act never locks), closing the one ungated edit path ([[decisions/2026-06-07-atlas-act-tier-shell-beforeload-guards]]). `tsc` EXIT 0; bounded vitest 67/67; live DOM probes confirmed Plan Tier-0 workbench (no map/tray), Plan non-Tier-0 map+tray revert, Act Tier-0 execution-only. **Committed `2d564e1d`** (10 files, +336/-136) on `main`, not pushed; the parallel guild/plan-data WIP (`actToolCatalog.ts`, `DesignElementLayers.tsx`, `objectiveActTools.ts`, one `keepAbovePrefix` line in `ActTierShell`) left unstaged ([[project-structured-capture-on-main]]). Amanah: pure IA/placement move, verbatim `scopeNotes` byte-untouched, no sale/advance-purchase/CSRA/salam ([[fiqh-csra-erased-2026-05-04]], [[feedback-csa-in-catalogues]]). Entities [[entities/act-tier-shell]], [[entities/plan-tier-shell]]; Log [[log/2026-06-11-atlas-workbench-act-to-plan]].
- [2026-06-11 Plan tier shell: Plan adopts Act's 4-rail map-centric layout, promoted to default](decisions/2026-06-11-atlas-plan-tier-shell-adoption.md) -- Operator: "I'd like for the Plan stage to adopt the UI layout of the Act stage." `ActTierShell` is a convergence of Plan's two legacy shells (`module-bar`, `stratum-spine`) into one map-centric 4-rail view; **Decision:** build `PlanTierShell` mirroring it 1:1 and default `getPlanShellMode` to `'tier-shell'` so every project opens on it -- same promote-without-deleting mechanism Act used ([[feedback-no-deletion]]: legacy branches stay in `PlanLayout`, toggle-reachable). The **one divergence from Act**: center mounts Plan's **editable** `VisionLayoutCanvas`/`DesignElementLayers`/`PlanDrawHost`/`PlanPhaseTabs` (Act read-only); right rail = `ObjectiveDetailPanel` with `hideMap` (map only in center); spine/objective via the **locking** engines `computeAllStratumStates`+`computeAllObjectiveStatuses`, NOT Act's never-lock rollup. NEW `planToolCatalog.ts` adds a Plan-only `'modules'` category (arm `'module'` -> `PlanModuleSlideUp`) atop `ACT_TOOL_CATEGORIES`; reuses Act chrome via two additive defaulted props (`ActTierObjectiveRail.hideModeToggle`, `ActTierSpine.ariaLabel`), Act byte-unchanged. **Verified:** shellModes 17/17, tsc clean; all three Plan shells render (legacy checked on builtin `mtc` -- server-synced 351 House reverts local `planShellMode` via WS re-sync); screenshot BLOCKED by deterministic map-mount preview hang ([[project-screenshot-hang]]), DOM/vitest fallback. Shipped commit `56b8170b` (9 files, +1179/-29) on `main`, not pushed; 4 parallel guild-WIP files left untouched ([[project-structured-capture-on-main]]). Amanah: pure layout/IA, no capital/sale/financing surface, no riba/gharar/CSRA/salam ([[fiqh-csra-erased-2026-05-04]], [[feedback-csa-in-catalogues]]). Mirrors [[decisions/2026-05-30-atlas-act-tier-shell-promotion]]; entity [[entities/plan-tier-shell]]; Log: [[log/2026-06-11-atlas-plan-tier-shell]].
- [2026-06-10 s2-ecology-c1 vegetation survey becomes a draw-on-map community survey with auto-%](decisions/2026-06-10-atlas-vegetation-survey-draw.md) -- The vegetation decision made the steward toggle 7 community types and hand-type a percent-of-site in the map-less Tier-0 workbench -- guesswork with no spatial record. The operator asked for a draw-on-map workflow where the right rail lists the 7 communities, the bottom tray offers a polygon draw tool, and percentages are computed automatically as `summed polygon acres / site acres * 100`. **Decision:** reuse the store-driven rail-takeover pattern (SectorsEditor / as-built precedent) -- `vegetationSurveyStore.open(projectId)` flips an ephemeral `active` flag, `ActTierShell` forces the map branch and swaps in `VegetationSurveyPanel`. Three operator-confirmed choices: (1) **draw-only, % auto** (manual entry removed for `mode === 'vegetation'` only; other 4 ecology subtasks unchanged); (2) **dedicated survey layer** -- NEW `vegetationSurveyStore` ("observed existing vegetation"), NOT the Plan `designElementsStore`, synced `ogden-vegetation-survey` v1 (coverage-guard test enforces registration); (3) **single `act.ecology.veg-survey` tool + in-panel community picker** (store carries `activeCommunity`; the sibling slope survey later inverted this to six per-class tools with no `activeClass` -- both patterns coexist). **Consequences:** `selectVegetationSurveyTotals` is the pure auto-% selector (`pct = siteAcres>0 ? (acres/siteAcres)*100 : 0`, divide-by-zero guarded; `unclassifiedPct = clamp(100-Sum, >=0)`); `siteAcres` from `project.location.acreage`; on "Done" totals encode back into the existing `ecologyCommunities` FormValue so the Tier-3 zone feed + summary are untouched; the draft-sync effect fires only when `features.length > 0` so empty surveys never clobber legacy values; a new mutually-exclusive rail-takeover coexists with the sectors editor + as-built popover. Amanah: ecological land-reading / measurement only -- no riba, gharar, or sale/advance-purchase/CSRA/salam framing ([[fiqh-csra-erased-2026-05-04]], [[feedback-csa-in-catalogues]]). Log: [[log/2026-06-10-atlas-vegetation-survey-draw]]; entity [[entities/act-tier-shell]].
- [2026-06-10 s2-terrain-c2 slope distribution becomes a draw-on-map survey with six per-class tools](decisions/2026-06-10-atlas-slope-survey-draw-tools.md) -- The slope decision made the steward hand-type a percentage per slope class (6 classes summing to ~100) -- guesswork divorced from terrain. The vegetation survey (`s2-ecology-c1`) had already shipped a full draw-on-map precedent (persisted `byProject` polygon store + ephemeral rail-takeover flag, DrawHost, map Layer, right-rail Panel, inline Summary, 7 integration touch-points), so the operator asked for the same treatment. **Two design questions confirmed before building:** (1) **six per-class bottom-rail draw tools** (`act.terrain.slope-flat` ... `slope-extreme`), not a veg-style single tool + in-panel picker -- the armed map tool itself encodes the class, so the store has **no `activeClass`** (unlike `vegetationSurveyStore`); `SlopeSurveyDrawHost` reads the armed tool at completion via `SLOPE_CLASS_BY_TOOL`, panel rows are a convenience second arming surface; (2) **% of total site area** (each class % = drawn acres / `project.location.acreage`) with an "Unclassified / not yet surveyed" remainder = `max(0, 100 - sum)` -- so the six %s don't sum to 100 until the whole site is drawn, and the slope branch of `isTerrainValid` is **relaxed** from `|sum - 100| <= 2` to `slopeSum > 0`. Drawing automates **only** the class % allocation; the compass `aspects` field stays a manual inline multi-select. Because `DecisionWorkingPanel` passes `onChange={setDraft}` (whole-FormValue replace), every summary write emits both `terrainSlope` + `terrainAspects`, and the slope-sync effect runs only when >= 1 polygon exists so legacy hand-typed values are never clobbered. **Consequences:** `terrainSlope` still encodes `['flat::30', ...]` (`encode/decodeTerrain`/`summariseTerrain` unchanged, honest for partial coverage); the six `slope-*` catalogue ids surface in the bottom tray only while the slope takeover forces the map for `s2-terrain`; slope polygons live in their own `slopeSurveyStore` / map layer (NOT the Plan `designElementsStore`), synced as `ogden-slope-survey` (persist v1, `byProject` only); a third mutually-exclusive rail-takeover now exists (veg / sectors / slope + the as-built popover). Aspect drawing + vertex-edit of existing slope polygons stay out of scope. Amanah: topographic land-reading / measurement only -- no riba, gharar, or ethical exposure. Log: [[log/2026-06-10-atlas-slope-survey-draw-tools]]; entity [[entities/act-tier-shell]].
- [2026-06-09 Tier-1+ decision mode badges: label-on-item, not a key->label map](decisions/2026-06-09-atlas-tier1plus-mode-badges.md) -- The Tier-0 `.mb-*` capture-mode chip (produced by `DecisionList`'s `modeFor` raw-key resolver + central `MODE_LABELS`, which also routes a bespoke panel) never rendered for Tier-1+ decisions; Tier-1+ has no bespoke captures, so there a mode badge is purely decorative. **Two forks settled:** (1) render on BOTH Tier-1+ surfaces (read-only Plan `DecisionChecklist` + interactive Act `ActTierExecutionPanel`) via one shared `ModeBadge.tsx` (co-located with Plan, imported by Act; identical markup + `mode-badge-<itemId>` testid), Tier-0 `DecisionList` path untouched (zero regression); (2) source the text as a VERBATIM label string on the catalogue item -- new optional `mode?: string` (`z.string().min(1).optional()`) threaded through `ck()`'s opts bag -- NOT a raw-key->label map and NOT component switch functions (Tier-1+ badges are bespoke-per-item, so a map would be ~1:1 indirection). **Rationale:** consistency with the catalogue-driven plan model (one objective drives Plan+Act from data); additive + absent-safe (every existing item validates unchanged); verbatim transcription preserves fidelity + Amanah (no silent rewording of financial/sale-channel phrasing). **Consequences:** 35 ecovillage badges authored across 6 prototyped objectives (others get none -- no fabricated data); badge is decoration only (no Tier-1+ panel routing -- deferred); two mode mechanisms coexist by design (Tier-0 `modeFor` key vs Tier-1+ `item.mode` label); re-order safety via per-objective representative-mode assertions. Shipped commit `734282ea` (8 files) on `main`. Amanah: ev-s4-financial-model badge copy = member cost-sharing, reviewed CLEAN 2026-06-08, no riba/`bay' ma laysa 'indak`/CSRA/salam ([[fiqh-csra-erased-2026-05-04]], [[feedback-csa-in-catalogues]]). Log: [[log/2026-06-09-atlas-tier1plus-mode-badges]]; entity [[entities/act-tier-shell]].
- [2026-06-09 OLOS UI/UX trust copy: central copy module + 10 mentor-register rewords](decisions/2026-06-09-olos-uiux-copy-module.md) -- Implemented all 10 trust-building UI/UX suggestions from `OLOS_UIUX_Suggestions.md` (theme "This Thinks The Way I Think") across the v3 Plan -> Act -> Observe surfaces, extracting every reworded user-facing string into a NEW central copy module `apps/web/src/v3/copy/` (barrel + `plan`/`act`/`observe`/`shared` + tests). **Operator-locked scope:** all 10 / "copy + light wiring" (defer genuinely new data work) / extract to a copy module. The module lives in **`apps/web`, NOT `packages/shared`** (it is React-surface chrome; shared stays UI-string-free): static strings -> frozen consts (mirrors the existing `HEADLINE`/`STATUS_LABEL` idiom); parameterized copy -> pure store-free unit-testable functions (`revisionHeadline(priority,cycleTitle?)`, `revisionSupporting({...})`, `domainUnansweredQuestion(domain)`, `feedsFallback(names)`, `observeSignalConfirmation(domainLabel|null)`, `decisionCount`); `DOMAIN_QUESTION` is a `Record<UniversalDomain,string>` exhaustive over all 16 domains (compiler- AND test-enforced). **Seed-data boundary held** -- structural `feedsInto` + authored per-item `feedHint`/`feedNote` stay in `packages/shared/src/constants/plan/`; only chrome templates (the `"Feeds {names}"` fallback) moved. Suggestion 4 reuses the existing `appendObserveFeedFor` emission (FieldAction has no `domainId` -> `null` confirmation); suggestion 6 terrain auto-detection + suggestion 10 future-cycle metrics + suggestion 4 cross-surface highlight **deferred** (recorded). - [2026-06-08 Live-site login bypass via per-visitor auto-registered demo sessions](decisions/2026-06-08-atlas-demo-mode-per-visitor-sessions.md) -- Live login (`atlas.ogden.ag`) is broken and the operator wants no login gate between test users and the app. Backend enforces JWT on nearly every route with no env bypass, so removing the frontend gate alone would 401 everywhere. **Decision:** behind a build-time flag `FEATURE_DEMO_MODE` (default off; on only for the live web build), on boot with no token, silently auto-register a unique throwaway account (`guest-<uuid>@demo.ogden.ag`) via the already-open `register` endpoint (7-day JWT) -- **zero backend changes**; the persisted token redirects the visitor straight into the app with the seeded "351 House" sample. Three operator sub-decisions: **auto demo session** (lands straight in), **keep login reachable** (shell shows a "DEMO MODE" badge + "Sign in" -> `/login`), **per-visitor throwaway accounts**. Entirely flag-gated -> terser folds OFF to false + dead-code-eliminates the demo path, so **OFF == original behavior by construction**; flag threaded `render.yaml` env -> Dockerfile build-arg -> Vite `define`. **Verified:** two fresh prod builds previewed with a temporary `preview.proxy` (reverted) -- bundle fold ON `!0` / OFF `!1`; demo-ON E2E (auto-register, DEMO MODE badge + Sign in, 351 House sample, no 401s -- screenshot), demo-OFF regression (no auto-register, public landing, no badge -- screenshot); 11 bounded unit tests; web `tsc` clean. Deferred: DB cleanup job for `@demo.ogden.ag` users, optional verification-email skip, the underlying real-login fix. Files: NEW `apps/web/src/app/demoSession.ts` (+test), `bootAuthed.ts`, `AppShell.tsx`+`.module.css`, `vite.config.ts`, `.env.example`, `infrastructure/Dockerfile.nginx`, `render.yaml`, `.claude/launch.json`. no persist-version bump (metadata already in `LocalProject`); (RW4) one-line hook in `ActTierShell.handleFormDataSave` gated on `formId === 's1-vision-steward'` (tsc-only per BT7/SW precedent). **Verified:** shared `tsc` EXIT 0; web `tsc` (8GB heap) no new errors outside pre-existing FOREIGN `designElementsStore.ts` WIP (two "Duplicate identifier 'widthM'" -- not mine); bounded `--pool=forks --testTimeout=20000` ([[feedback-vitest-bounded-runs]]) RW1 schema (5) + RW2 mapper (4; - [2026-06-06 Tier-0 Vision-classify surface (Phase C Part 2: bespoke committed/aspirational sort)](decisions/2026-06-06-atlas-tier0-vision-classify.md) -- Replaced the **generic** `VisionFormFields` rendering of the `s1-vision-classify` Tier-0 decision with a **bespoke surface** that sorts candidate **vision elements** into two columns -- **Committed** (do now) vs **Aspirational** (longer-horizon) -- via type-aware suggestion chips, a **transient Unclassified staging zone**, a write-your-own input with a committed/aspirational role toggle, in-column switch/delete, and a show-more toggle. Follows the Phase-B `SuccessCriteriaCapture` + Phase-C-Part-1 `LabourInventoryCapture` controlled-renderer pattern (reuses, does NOT rebuild, the Tier-0 workbench/panel). **Decision (additive, no deletion):** (1) **byte-compatible value -- NO encode** -- the value shape `{ committed: string[]; aspirational: string[] }` is already NATIVE `FormValue` (both arms plain `string[]`, the SAME shape the existing form tool persists), so `decodeClassify` is a TOTAL read (non-array -> `[]`; non-string elements filtered, `[1,null,'x'] -> ['x']`) with no inverse encode, `onChange` writes the two arrays straight back; (2) **transient Unclassified staging is component-local UI, NEVER persisted** -- a staged chip lives only in `useState` until the steward sorts it into a column, `inUse(text)` enforces text-uniqueness across all three lists; (3) **type-aware suggestions via shared `resolveVisionClassifyOptions(primary, secondaries)`** (mirrors the `resolveLabourSkills`/`resolveSuccessCriteriaOptions` union/dedup/order idiom; starter `VISION_CLASSIFY_OPTIONS` REVIEW-flagged) -- **plain strings, NOT domain-tagged** (the committed/aspirational axis is the steward's sort-time judgement, not a design-time tag); (4) **bespoke validity/summary routed FIRST** (before labour/success-criteria/`hasFields`/textarea) -- `isVisionClassifyValid` (`committed.length + aspirational.length >= 1`) + `summariseVisionClassify` ("N committed, M aspirational"), NOT the generic `isFormValueValid`/`summariseFormValue`; the draft is decoded ONCE into a single `classifyModel` reused by validity/summary/body (mirrors labour `labourModel`); the early arm is **load-bearing** because `s1-vision-classify` DOES match a form tool (would otherwise fall through to the generic renderer); (5) detection via `buildDecisionTarget` flagging `isVisionClassify` directly through `item.id === 's1-vision-classify'` (simpler than labour's tool-formId join, dependency-free), workbench resolves suggestions inline (no-memo) + threads them via the new `visionClassifySuggestions` panel prop (the vision-classify form tool + its `fields` stay in `actToolCatalog.ts` as the modal/`<select>` fallback). **Verified:** shared `tsc` clean; final whole-implementation review (Part 1 + Part 2) + live smoke tracked next under the consolidated Phase-C plan (Phase-B map-flicker fix `a842f3f2` makes the smoke viable). Four mockup blocks: WHO single-select (4 cards), weekly HOURS stepper + capacity-band signal, SEASONAL steppers + annual-rhythm viz, type-aware SKILLS list. **Decision (additive, no deletion):** (1) **bespoke controlled renderer over a FLAT `FormValue`** -- the component reasons with a rich `LabourModel` but persists the UNCHANGED `FormValue` type `{ who, hours, spring, summer, autumn, winter: string; skills: string[] }` (each skill `name::level`); component-owned `encode`/`decode` round-trip losslessly, `decode` is TOTAL (defaults for missing/garbage; unknown level -> `beginner`; `NaN` hours -> `0`) and splits each skill on the LAST `::` so custom names containing `::` round-trip; (2) **display-default baking** -- `decode` never fabricates data, the COMPONENT applies the mockup display fallbacks (hours `20`; seasonal `25/20/30/10`) only when unset and bakes them on first edit, Record disabled until the user affirms; (4) **bespoke validity/summary routed BEFORE `hasFields`** -- `isLabourValid` (who set AND `hours > 0` AND `>= 1` skill) + `summariseLabour` (e.g. "Small paid team, 20 hrs/wk, 4 skills"), NOT the generic `isFormValueValid`/`summariseFormValue`; (5) detection via `buildDecisionTarget` flagging `isLabourInventory` when `formId === 's1-vision-labour'`, workbench resolves skills inline (no-memo) + threads them via the new `labourSkillSuggestions` panel prop (the labour form tool + its `fields` stay in `actToolCatalog.ts` as the modal/`<select>` fallback). **Verified:** shared `tsc` clean; - [2026-06-05 Act-stage per-protocol threshold editor](decisions/2026-06-05-atlas-act-protocol-threshold-editor.md) -- **(SUPERSEDED on placement by the relocation ADR above -- the editor now lives in Plan, not Act; the store/hook/editor internals below still hold.)** Lets a steward adjust, from the Act protocol detail pane, the bracketed `[token]` thresholds in a standing protocol's trigger condition (e.g. `[reserve threshold]` in "IF stored water falls below [reserve threshold]"). **Why:** `useProtocolLibrary` derived substitution `outputs` solely from the legacy `s6-yield-flows` `parameterGroup` (5 tokens) whose names **never intersect** the ~32 tokens in the resolved per-type Act catalogues -> every Act condition rendered a verbatim, uneditable bracket (widening the parameterGroup is blocked by `protocolOutputs.test.ts`'s orphan guard). Triggering is manual (no eval engine), so the ask = make the **value substituted into the human-read condition** editable. Operator decisions (AskUserQuestion): value scope = **per-protocol** (`(projectId, templateId, token)`); coverage = **full now** (additive persisted slice covering ANY `[token]` in ANY active protocol); edit UX = **inline live-persist**. **Strategy A (additive):** new `planStratumStore.protocolTokenOverridesByProject` slice + `setProtocolTokenOverride`/`clearProtocolTokenOverrides` + stable frozen-empty `selectProjectProtocolOverrides`; additive v5->v6 backfill migration, `partialize`+`cloneForProject` extended; no record/condition shape change -> legacy S6 path, Plan ParameterGroup, shared catalogues + orphan guard untouched. `useProtocolLibrary` returns memoised `outputsFor(templateId) = {...outputs, ...(overrides[templateId] ?? {})}` (base ref when no overrides -> Plan columns byte-unaffected). New `ActProtocolThresholdEditor.tsx` exports pure `extractConditionTokens` (deduped first-seen via `renderConditionSegments(condition, {})`), `null` when no tokens, else one input/token (per-keystroke persist) + conditional `Reset`; subscribes inline via `s.protocolTokenOverridesByProject[pid]?.[tid]` (indexes, never derives -> no Zustand v5 loop); `ActProtocolDetailPane`/`ProtocolLayerPanel` render via `outputsFor(id)` so the IF/THEN substitutes live. **Verified:** web `tsc` EXIT 0 (8GB heap; caught + fixed a real `template.title`->`template.name`); 19/19 bounded `--pool=forks` (`planStratumStore.protocolOverrides` (12) + `ActProtocolThresholdEditor` via full `ActProtocolDetailPane` (7)). Live DOM proof + **screenshot** on MTC S5 `u-s5-water-store-low`: typing "20% of capacity" substituted live into the card IF (gold), Reset returned `[reserve threshold]` + hid the control, store net-zero; no-token `u-s3-flow-anomaly-reassess` mounted the pane but NO editor ([[project-screenshot-hang]]). Explicit-path commit `b79f8f50` (7 files, +759/-7; foreign `ActOpsDashboard`/`ActTierShell`/`ActTierWeatherPanel*`/`_tsc_review.txt`/wiki WIP unstaged); 0 behind / no divergence; not pushed ([[project-branch-rebase]]); CSRA untouched. - [2026-06-04 OLOS local-first Phase 2 -- generic record WS broadcast + reconnect delta-pull](decisions/2026-06-04-olos-local-first-record-broadcast-reconnect-delta.md) -- Phase 2 of plan `the-goal-is-to-bright-blanket` (local-first hardening for a 2-6 trusted field team; full days offline = normal case; field-hub deploy + CRDT out of scope). Closed the live + catch-up real-time gaps for the four typed-record Act stores (`ogden-field-actions`/`ogden-observe-feed`/`ogden-observe-data-points`/`ogden-observe-cycles`), all on the single generic `synced_records` PUT transport, each row carrying its own monotonic `rev`+`updated_at`. **Decided:** ONE generic `record_upserted`/`record_deleted` WsEvent pair (drop non-strictly-newer `rev`), not one-per-domain; server broadcasts author-excluded on the PUT; a SINGLE guarded client apply `applyIncomingRecord` shared by the live WS handler AND the reconnect delta-pull, owning per-record `rev` bookkeeping + three guards (rev/echo => author never double-applies own echo; version-skew drop+one-shot warn; init-clobber => pending un-synced local push never overwritten), applied inside `setSyncGuard`; a new `GET .../changed-since?since=<ISO>` endpoint + `pullActRecordDelta` that advances `lastSyncedAt` to the **newest server `updated_at`** (clock-skew-immune) and runs FIRST in `onOnline` so an idle all-day-offline device still catches up; `record_deleted` log-and-skip (upsert-only wire, no generic remove hook); olos observations/proofs broadcasts deferred (separate tables, no registry-routable consumer). **Caveats:** `reconcileOnReconnect` activated (now re-fetches features+comments on WS re-open); `onOnline` client-now `setLastSyncedAt` can clobber the server watermark (accepted -- re-pull is `rev`-idempotent). Gated behind `FEATURE_SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` (default OFF). 4 commits `d2fd8930`/`2298eceb`/`6d4619d7`/`4d8f3b7a`; 9/9 + 8/8 sibling vitest green (`--pool=forks`); web tsc EXIT 0; two-browser live test operator-run; not pushed ([[project-branch-rebase]]). - [2026-06-03 Cross-protocol co-occurrence detection -- derived read-model on Plan + Observe](decisions/2026-06-03-atlas-cooccurrence-detection.md) -- The "north star" follow-on to the protocol-deviation Review-flag feature: when >= 2 DISTINCT protocols each hold an OPEN flag in the same `season:cycle` bucket, surface a single **root-cause-collapse verdict** (the deep design assumption sits below what the design assumed), not N isolated chips. Keys on co-DEVIATION not co-firing; interpretation DERIVED from the constituent flags' `depth` + objectives (+ ihsan overlay for `emergency-destocking`); a derived VIEW over open flags (no new store / persist / lifecycle -- dissolves when flags resolve); one `useCoOccurrenceClusters` hook feeds an actionable Plan banner + a read-only Observe card. Conservative grouping (exclude `cycleNumber===undefined`; >= 2 distinct `sourceTemplateId`). Shell banner omits `currentBucket` by design (cross-stratum has no single domain/cycle; season-only bucket is a verified `isFlagDormantByWindow` no-op). **T1-T4 shipped** (`37ff5502`,`7e809728`,`f0cb88ce`,`0c85ceda`): shared detection, hook, banner, Plan-shell mount. Web tsc EXIT 0; T3 component test green. **T4 caveat:** the full-shell mount test HANGS (router/store surface intractable to mock) so it was NOT committed -- integration rests on tsc + the T3 test + the deferred T6 preview gate. **T5 (Observe card) + T6 (preview gate + persist) PENDING.** Not pushed. - [2026-06-03 Observation log -- append-only per-flag-closure ledger (slice #2)](decisions/2026-06-03-atlas-observation-log.md) -- The historical substrate for chronic detection. Slice #1's co-occurrence verdict is a derived VIEW over OPEN flags and dissolves when they resolve, losing the past. This slice records it: a headless, persisted, append-only ledger of review-flag CLOSURE events (resolve + dismiss), emitted at the lowest chokepoint (INSIDE `reviewFlagStore.resolveFlag`/`dismissFlag`, never the UI). Per-flag-closure grain (NOT per-cluster -- the log never knows what a cluster is; the chronic detector reconstructs clusters by grouping rows across cycles). Append-only twin of `proofEventStore` (`records[]`, `append`, persist `ogden-observation-log` v1, no update/remove, unbounded retention). Persisted => zod-validated `ObservationLogRecord` + pure `buildObservationLogRecord`; `acknowledgeFlag`/dormancy/re-open emit nothing; reopen-reclose logs two. Naming deviation: `ObservationLogRecord` (not `ObservationRecord`, which collides with an unrelated Observe-objective barrel export). T1-T4 (`5bd16828`,`66b881f1`,`ae4286d9`) shipped + preview-verified (`preview_eval`, screenshot unavailable [[project-screenshot-hang]]). Not pushed. Builds on [[decisions/2026-06-03-atlas-cooccurrence-detection]]; consumed by the chronic-detection entry below; entities [[entities/protocols-dashboard]] + [[entities/observe-dashboard]]; Log: [[log/2026-06-03-atlas-observation-log]].
- [2026-06-03 Chronic / multi-cycle co-occurrence detector (slice #3)](decisions/2026-06-03-atlas-chronic-detection.md) -- Unions slice #1's live OPEN clusters (present) with slice #2's CLOSED flag ledger (past) to surface **chronic structural verdicts**: the same protocol template PAIR co-deviating in the SAME season across >= 2 distinct cycles = a structural design FAILURE (redesign, not retune). **Per-PAIR verdict atom** (NOT connected-component merge -- that would over-claim {A,B}@c1,2 + {B,C}@c3,4 as one {A,B,C} spanning 1-4); **season-scoped** (spring water-stress != autumn); "consecutive" is a sort modifier, not a hard gate; union by (season, cycleNumber) one occurrence per cycle; undated excluded; per-template attribution inside a bucket (a flat aggregate leaked a 3rd template's attrs into a pair -- the T3.1 code-quality catch, fixed via per-template Map + regression tests); derived view (no zod); deterministic tuple sort, existential/ihsan first. Stable cross-store `useChronicVerdicts` (two Zustand roots + one useMemo + EMPTY_VERDICTS) feeds a NEW actionable Plan banner `ChronicVerdictBanner` + a NEW read-only Observe card `ChronicSynthesisCard` (shipped slice-#1 components untouched -- siblings). **Retention AMENDS the slice-#2 unbounded-retention covenant**: steward-initiated, observable, chronic-aware `pruneProjectRecords` + pure `partitionExpiredRecords` (keep undated OR within season's most-recent 12 distinct cycles OR chronic-protected; returns pruned; NO auto-trigger). **Known bounded limitation:** prune-protection is ledger-only, so a verdict detectable solely via a still-OPEN live cluster isn't prune-protected until that flag closes (low-risk; default window keeps recent legs; disclosed not hidden). T3.1-T3.6 (`9aae593f`,`fa51aaf5`,`47e603a7`,`d344bf23`,`c9a33381`,`df6405d9`) shipped; shared 51/51 + web 78/78 bounded-forks green; slice-3 files tsc-clean (foreign commit `29662ef3` catalogue + import-only spine carry pre-existing tsc errors, recorded); live preview gate via `preview_eval` (screenshot unavailable [[project-screenshot-hang]], DATA-path verified). Not pushed. Act's log form writes the store; Observe (Unified + Curve + Phase) reads it, so a manual reading flows into the curve, phase detection, and pathogen-kill (>= 3 consecutive days >= 55 C). Gate screenshot-verified (64 C logged -> 147 F -> Observe 63.9 C, Days Pasteurising 12, Pathogen Kill CONFIRMED). Phases: P1 `bf9e7853`, P2 `e26d6550`, P3 `c7ec380f`; P4 deferred. - [2026-05-29 projectType normalization: stop project:create 422ing on sync](decisions/2026-05-29-atlas-projecttype-normalization-422-fix.md) -- Continuation of [[decisions/2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-coalescing-fix]] on `feat/atlas-permaculture` (commit `fe367966`, 3 files). That fix bounded the sync queue so a permanently-failing op could no longer OOM the renderer; this fix removes the *cause* of the validation failures and names it. OLOS carries two project-type vocabularies -- kebab-case **archetype** (`regenerative-farm`, `trueNorthConfig.ts`) and the snake_case server **`projectType`** (`regenerative_farm`, the Zod `ProjectType` enum); `createProject` persisted the raw value, so a kebab archetype could leak into `projectType` and `project:create` 422'd on sync, the circuit breaker dropping the op (unsyncable on-device). **Three-tier fix:** `normalizeProjectType()` maps kebab archetypes via `ARCHETYPE_TO_PROJECT_TYPE` / passes valid enum values / nulls unknowns (syncable); `createProject` normalizes on write (prevent); persist `migrate` v4 -> v5 repairs existing records (repair); `describeSyncError()` folds the server `details: [{ path, message }]` into `op.lastError` + the create-failure log (diagnose -- so the next 422 names the field instead of the opaque "Request validation failed"). Live diagnosis named the offender as **"Phase 4 Smoke"** (`regenerative-farm`), correcting the 2026-05-25 ADR's provisional "Moontrance Creek" / "Test Vision Project" attribution (a dated correction callout was added there; "Test Vision Project" was a transient vision-builder fixture [[decisions/2026-05-25-atlas-stage-zero-vision-builder]], Moontrance Creek is `projectType: null` / valid). Verified: web `tsc --noEmit` clean; live `ogden-projects` migrated to version 5 with 0 schema offenders across 40 projects, clean projects untouched. Deferred (corrected 2026-05-29): the handler-swallow item was already closed the same day by [[decisions/2026-05-25-atlas-sync-circuit-breaker]] (`84bb8e91`) -- `executeQueuedOp` rethrows so `flush()` counts retries and drops exhausted ops via `handleExhaustedOp`. Genuinely-open deferral: the human-gated two-device E2E + `FEATURE_SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` rollout. CSRA model untouched; ASCII-only copy. Log: [[log/2026-05-29-projecttype-normalization-422-fix]].
- [2026-05-28 Slice 5.5a: Role substrate + access foundation (bulk role map + Per-Project Home access gate + Portfolio role badge + contractor 403)](decisions/2026-05-28-slice-55a-role-substrate.md) — Shipped the first slice of the scoped-views epic on `feat/atlas-permaculture` across explicit-path commits (`8e67b15` shared alias break -> `e5c99da` api endpoint -> `6534d11` apiClient + store -> `5a2b74e` hook -> `74d85a2` home gate -> `51af727` portfolio badge): the role substrate end to end. New `GET /api/v1/projects/my-roles` returns the caller's role per non-builtin project (mirrors the `GET /projects` list query); `memberStore.fetchMyRoles` folds it into a server-id-keyed record; `useMyProjectRoles` exposes a `ReadonlyMap<serverId, ProjectRole>` that is empty and fetch-free when signed out, so the dominant offline/demo flow always renders the full single-owner view. That one map is the single role source for both new surfaces: the **Per-Project Home access gate** (a contractor or landowner on a SYNCED project gets an honest empty state instead of the steward home — their task / portal surfaces ship in 5.5c / 5.5d) and the **Portfolio role badge** (non-steward roles get a small badge; owner / primary_steward get none; no card is ever hidden). The gate reads the bulk map by `serverId`, not the singular `useProjectRole` slot, so cross-project navigation never flashes an owned project's home as denied with a stale role. **Enforcement spine:** `ROLE_ALIAS.contractor` flipped `'designer' -> null` — since every Plan/Observe/Act mutation gate shares `requireRole('owner','designer')`, this single lever denies contractor at all of them (403); the fine-grained capability map is untouched (two-axis design), and scoped Act access is re-granted with assignment-scoping in 5.5c (between 5.5a and 5.5c a contractor has no functional surface — correct, the surface ships in 5.5c). Verified: shared + web vitest green (alias contract with 4 flipped contractor assertions + focused contractor-no-gate test, store transform, hook no-op-offline, home gate, card badge); shared/web/api `tsc --noEmit` clean; `my-roles` 401-unauthenticated smoke (route registered + gated; Postgres-backed integration test deferred with rationale — query mirrors the shipping list query); offline-portfolio screenshot confirms no badges signed out. No-deletion; 3-item nav forward IA ([[project-lifecycle-retirement]]); CSRA model untouched; ASCII-only copy. Implements [[decisions/2026-05-28-atlas-scoped-views-epic-design]]; log [[log/2026-05-28-slice-55a-role-substrate]].
- [2026-05-28 Scoped Views Epic (Phase 5 Slice 5.5 re-scoped: Contractor / Landowner / Team-member scoped Project Home)](decisions/2026-05-28-atlas-scoped-views-epic-design.md) — **Design record on `feat/atlas-permaculture`; no implementation code yet.** Re-scopes the one-line "Slice 5.5 — Contractor/Landowner scoped views, frontend-only, hook signature unchanged" carry-over (from the 5.3/5.4 ADRs) into a **four-slice epic** after the ratified `OLOS_Project_Home_Spec_v1` (sections 1.3/4/5/6/7/8) was read in full against the code. The literal carry-over collapsed on three walls: (1) `memberStore.myRole` is a single slot — no per-project role map to filter a portfolio on; (2) `useProjectRole` only fetches when logged in + Portfolio Home reads the localStorage store, so a naive role filter empties the portfolio in the dominant offline/demo mode; (3) frontend filtering is not the spec's data-layer 403 (sections 7.2/8.5). Two findings de-risk it: the API already gates ~every route on `authenticate -> resolveProjectRole -> requireRole(...)` (~22 callsites per `rbac.ts`), and the landowner view has a real foundation in the existing `v3/observe/.../presentation/` suite + `presentationShareStore` + the `portal/` public-link API. **Locked principle (AskUserQuestion):** scoped views are an **authenticated + synced** capability — local-only / offline projects always render full single-owner view (rejected: mandatory backend-backing; mirroring roles into the local store). Sharpest enforcement finding: `contractor` currently aliases to `designer` (`projectRoleCapabilities.ts:158`) with `{read,comment,edit}` over the whole project, so a contractor session satisfies every `requireRole('owner','designer')` gate today — Slice 5.1 flagged this as a deliberate placeholder; 5.5a/5.5c own breaking it (403 on Plan/Observe + scope to assigned field actions). **Roadmap:** 5.5a role substrate + enforcement spine (`useMyProjectRoles` bulk hook + Per-Project Home access gate + Portfolio role-filter no-op offline + contractor 403) -> 5.5b team-member scoped home -> 5.5c contractor task-only view -> 5.5d landowner read-only progress view + contractor access expiry. View order Team -> Contractor -> Landowner chosen for a steady risk ramp. **Immediate next:** Slice 5.5a implementation plan + execution. Hook signature unchanged (the one surviving piece of the original carry-over); no-deletion; 3-item nav forward IA; CSRA model untouched; ASCII-only copy. Log: [[log/2026-05-28-scoped-views-epic-design]]; continues [[decisions/2026-05-28-atlas-per-project-home-slice54]].

- [2026-05-25 Bound the Command Centre shell grid (definite height + clamped column)](decisions/2026-05-25-atlas-command-centre-shell-bounding.md) — Fixes the Act Command Centre's bottom "Open Work Items" tray clipping at the viewport bottom **only** on the **All Modules / Tracker** tabs (a first carousel-only attempt `53a0e7a0` missed — the clip was the whole tray, not the carousel). Surface = the shared stage-agnostic `CommandCentreShell` (Observe/Plan/Act); `.shell` grid is the sole direct child of AppShell's `.main` (`flex:1; position:relative; overflow:hidden`). **Two `.shell` facts combined:** (1) `height:100%` didn't reliably bound the grid → auto-height → the `1fr` body row stretched to the **tallest column** (Act's tall right ops rail) and pushed the `auto` tray below the viewport where `.main{overflow:hidden}` clipped it (worst on the tallest-rail tabs; the carousel is horizontal so item count widens, not heightens); (2) no explicit grid **column** → implicit `auto` column grew to the widest row's max-content (long carousel/tab strip), blowing the body out (~9710px) and shoving the rail off-screen. **CSS-only fix in `.shell`:** `height:100%` → `position:absolute; inset:0` (definite height; grid clamps, sidebar/rail scroll internally, tray always visible) + add `grid-template-columns: minmax(0,1fr)`. One sheet fixes all three stages; covenant-clean (no JSX/store/schema/model/migration). Verified via live `preview_eval` (shell bounded 812px = `.main` height, rail on-screen, tray within viewport) **+ a confirming screenshot** of the full Act layout with intact Tracker cards. Commit `2368e687`. Log: [[log/2026-05-25-command-centre-shell-bounding]]. Continues [[log/2026-05-25-command-centre-tray-and-waterrouter-fixes]].
- [2026-05-25 Sync-queue circuit-breaker — propagate API failures so retries count and exhausted ops surface](decisions/2026-05-25-atlas-sync-circuit-breaker.md) — Closes the circuit-breaker deferred by the OOM fix. `flush()`'s retry/backoff/drop machinery only runs when the executor **throws**, but `executeQueuedOp` routed create/update through swallowing live-path handlers — a failing queued op never retried and (post coalescing-key) silently dropped after one pass. Fix: `rethrow=false` param on each swallowing create/update handler re-throws before re-enqueue; `executeQueuedOp` opts in; new `handleExhaustedOp` (wired as `flush()`'s `onDrop`) records a new `droppedStores` channel on `connectivityStore` + `toast.error`; `OfflineBanner` gains a highest-severity "could not be saved" banner. Live path unchanged. Phase 2 static audit: dormant `FLAGS.SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` full-coverage path fully wired + unit-verified (129/129); flagged `ogden-projects` double-classification for the E2E. Deferred (human-gated): two-device E2E + flag rollout. Verified: typecheck 0; 6 new + 123 existing sync tests green. Commit `84bb8e91`. Builds on [[decisions/2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-coalescing-fix]]; log [[log/2026-05-25-sync-circuit-breaker]].
- [2026-05-25 Bound the sync queue with a coalescing key to stop renderer OOM](decisions/2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-coalescing-fix.md) — Fixes a recurring Chrome "Aw, Snap! Out of Memory" on command-centre routes. Confirmed root cause (via a "Syncing 254520 changes…" screenshot, after refuting every in-render hypothesis by measurement): the IndexedDB sync queue (`syncQueue.ts`, `ogden-sync-queue`/`ops`) was an unbounded append log — `enqueue()` keyed ops by random UUID so the same failing entity re-queued forever (two local projects failing API validation on every push), and `flush()` loaded the whole queue via `getAll()` (250k ops × GeoJSON = multi-GB) into the JS heap. Fix: **coalescing deterministic key** `storeType:action:localId` (re-queue overwrites → growth structurally bounded); `getBatch(limit)` cursor read + `FLUSH_BATCH=200` instead of `getAll()`; `reconcile()` one-time cursor collapse run at `syncService.start()`; `flush()` now drops exhausted ops. Verified: 20k-op runaway reconciled to 5 with heap flat ~71–74 MB then drained to 0; typecheck exit 0. Deferred: circuit-breaker for the ~14 swallow-and-re-enqueue executor handlers. Commit `e5e8f220`. Hardens [[concepts/local-first-architecture]]; log [[log/2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-fix]].

Three scope calls: boundary → OBSERVE (intake captures only a name), module activation **preview-only** for MVP (strip shown but doesn't yet gate Plan/Act modules), full ~15-step set with conditionals (livestock/residential). - [2026-05-25 Conflict Detection + Plan Versioning + Synthesis/Approval (Plan-Operation Phase 5 — FINAL)](decisions/2026-05-25-atlas-plan-conflict-version-synthesis-phase5.md) — The **final** Plan-Operation roadmap slice, shipped as three commit-on-verify sub-slices on `feat/atlas-permaculture` (**5a** `72f9cabb` · **5b** `68b5f526` · **5c** `2b408b9b`). **5a — Plan Conflict Detection** (`/plan/conflicts`): closes the last dangling Observe↔Plan edge — a new recorded observation that contradicts an existing decision surfaces as a triageable conflict. Pure `derivePlanConflicts(views, decisions)` matches recorded/resolved observations to non-`rejected` decisions via module affinity (`likely`=direct, `possible`=affinity) + an optional separate turf point-in-polygon pass; thin-run triage (`dismiss|acknowledge|revise-plan`+note) in `ogden-plan-conflict-reviews` (mirrors Phase 1's derived-flag/stored-run split). **5b — Plan Versioning** (`/plan/versions`): full-geometry snapshot + restore. The engine combines the `syncManifest` `selectForProject`/`applyForProject` engine over ~63 versioned-blob stores (skipping `ogden-plan-versions` itself → no recursion) with a 4-store typed-design array adapter (zones/paths/utilities/built-environment-v2) the manifest omits; draft/approved/superseded lifecycle; `window.confirm`-gated Restore overwrites only this project's rows. **Testability fix:** `planSnapshot.ts` can't be imported under vitest (the `syncManifest→projectStore→cascadeDelete→useZoneStore` cycle + zundo/persist `zoneStore` crashes at load via `store.persist.getOptions()` undefined), so the bespoke project-slice filter/replace was extracted into a pure store-free `planSnapshotMerge.ts` and tested there (the genuine restore-safety invariant) — no production guard (would silence real rehydrate instrumentation), no DI refactor. **5c — Plan Synthesis & Approval** (`/plan/synthesis`): a read-mostly roll-up (readiness tiles + open items + active version, composing the existing counts hooks) plus an **advisory approval** stamp — Approve stamps a `PlanVersion` draft→approved (who/when/note) or captures a fresh snapshot; Reopen reverses it; steward-sovereign, locks/gates nothing; no new store (approval metadata on `PlanVersion`). Each slice added its route (before `plan/$module`) + a sidebar entry. Covenant clean (operational only — no riba/gharar/CSRA/salam/financing). Verified: 5b `planVersion.test.ts`(5)+`planSnapshot.test.ts`(7)+syncManifest guard **22/22**; 5a `planConflict.test.ts`+guard; `tsc` at the 3-error pre-existing baseline. Browser visual check deferred (auth-bypass forbidden). **Closes the Plan-Operation roadmap (Phases 1–5) — the living-plan loop is end-to-end.** Log: [[log/2026-05-25-plan-conflict-version-synthesis-phase5]]. Continues [[decisions/2026-05-25-atlas-plan-workspace-phase4]].

EMPTY_CHECKS, obj.nodes.length)` so the toast agrees with the panel pill exactly; toast components unchanged (`pct===100` gate correct once fed real numbers). - [2026-05-22 Atlas Phase C consolidation — Plan-stage authoring is PDC-complete (C1–C6)](decisions/2026-05-22-atlas-phase-c-consolidation.md) — **Umbrella ADR declaring Phase C complete.** Ties C1–C5 (`cf6fcbfc` paths · `f2607703` utility points · `15612b75` landDesign no-sync · `b498fe8a` canonical ownership + utility-point tool · `5ad3c3b4` edit parity + orientation) into **four named patterns**: (1) **canonical-ownership matrix** — one canonical store/tool per concern (paths/utility-points/BE-infra/connector-runs/freeform-sketch), enforced by what each tool offers, no data migration; (2) **typed-promotion pattern** — promoting a blob store onto typed `design_features` is a pure web-side mirror needing ZERO API/PDF-template change (mapper pair + `serverId?` + sync handlers + subscribe + merge block + `syncManifest` reclassify out of the blob loop), with C3 as the inverse safety lesson (a `typed-design-feature` classification with no transport wired syncs nothing); (3) **authoring-surface type-split** — resolve overlapping models (`utilityStore` 15 types vs BE V2) via a derived `UTILITY_POINT_TYPES = keys − BE_OWNED` partition, no persisted data moved; (4) **v3 edit-parity surface** — every PDC feature type (paths/structures/utility points) is click-to-edit on the canvas with a field set matching its draw form, plus the selected-structure orientation chevron. **C6 verification:** full Phase C unit surface green (C1 4/4 · C2 5/5 · C3 77 · C4 5/5 · C5 7/7) + web tsc at the 3-error pre-existing baseline + a live DOM regression check (seeded `/v3/project/mtc/plan` loads with a canvas, no C5 console errors — only the expected `:3001` API-down sync error). **Deferred (stated, not claimed):** the chevron *drawing* + edit-form *opening on click* + the live cross-device round-trip stay behind the auth + seeded-project (API down) + headless-WebGL + MapTiler + screenshot-hang wall; unit tests + tsc are the durable posture. **No persisted data migrated across all of Phase C** (transport/authoring only — stewardship sovereignty). With Phases A + B + C done, the three roadmap gaps blocking Atlas as the only PDC-portfolio tool are closed (Canvas + peer-review blog are the course LMS, intentionally out of scope). - [2026-05-22 Atlas canonical access/utility ownership + reach the C2 utility-point promotion (PDC Phase C, C4)](decisions/2026-05-22-atlas-canonical-feature-ownership-c4.md) — Closes the C4 deferral from the C1–C2 ADR. **The C2 utility-point promotion was unreachable:** `utilityStore` (typed `point` design_features, syncable, rosterable) had **no Plan draw tool** (`MapToolId` union lacked `utility-point`, `PlanDrawHost` had no case) and **no v3 render layer** (`PlanDataLayers` never imported `useUtilityStore`) — a utility point could be neither drawn nor seen even though C2 made it round-trip through sync. Also resolves the **overlapping-authoring** confusion between the two utility concepts: `builtEnvironmentStoreV2` (BE V2 — well/septic/tank/pump/solar + power/fence/gate/driveway, keyed by `state`, authored via `be.*`) vs `utilityStore` (15 types — **4 exact-duplicate BE kinds** + **11 with no BE equivalent**). **Locked steward decisions:** (1) C4 = clarity + wire the missing tool, **NOT a destructive migration** — no data moves; (2) **BE V2 is canonical** for the 6 overlapping infra kinds (per the 2026-05-10 BE-unification ADR); (3) the new tool offers **only the 11 non-BE types**, the 4 duplicates authored via `be.*`. **The type-split is the load-bearing mechanism, not a schema change:** a pure `utilityPointTypes.ts` (no React/maplibre deps, unit-testable in isolation) holds `BE_OWNED_UTILITY_TYPES` (the 4) + `UTILITY_POINT_TYPES` = `Object.keys(UTILITY_TYPE_CONFIG)` **minus** that set (derived, so a new `UtilityType` auto-buckets and the partition test catches an unclassified one) + `UTILITY_POINT_TYPE_OPTIONS`. New `UtilityPointTool.tsx` mirrors `WaterStorageTool` (`draw_point` → `addUtility` full record → `openForm`; fields type/name/demandKwhPerDay/capacityGal/phase, **no `enterprise`** — `Utility` has none; type-change autofills name only while still the prior default; `onSave` → `updateUtility`, cancel → `deleteUtility`). Wired into the `MapToolId` union (`useMapToolStore`), the **dedicated-store switch** in `PlanDrawHost` (bypasses `PLAN_BE_PREFIX` → mounts on **both Current + Vision** canvases, parity with `utility-run`), the `utility`-category rail in `PlanTools` (`Zap` icon, appended after the `BE_TOOL_GROUPS` map so it keeps its non-BE toolId), and `PlanDataLayers` (each `center` → shared `plan-data-point` source + label, props from `UTILITY_TYPE_CONFIG`; the point-click handler returns early on an unknown `kind` so full edit stays with the legacy `UtilityPanel`). `elementCatalog.ts` got a **clarity comment only** (no delete — removing kinds is a data risk). **Verification:** `utilityPointTypes.test.ts` 5/5 (BE_OWNED=the 4, UTILITY_POINT_TYPES=the 11, 15-way partition, never-offers-BE, option/label validity); web tsc at the 3-error pre-existing baseline (foreign `WasteVectorDashboardView.tsx` errors excluded from the by-name commit `b498fe8a`); **live DOM-level (Claude Preview :5200)** beyond the auth wall — seeded `/v3/project/mtc/plan` `hasCanvas:true`, the "Utility point" button renders in the Utilities category + click **mounts `UtilityPointTool`** (`aria-label="Utility point tool"` + draw hint); `preview_screenshot` timed out (known WebGL / backgrounded-tab hang) → **no visual claimed** per CLAUDE.md, DOM evals authoritative; live cross-device draw→reload→roster e2e **deferred** (stated, not claimed) behind the Phase A/B/C wall. Covenant clean — no public capital framing touched; no persisted data migrated (stewardship sovereignty). **Deferred:** C5 (structure `rotationDeg` + orientation indicator), C6 (full e2e + consolidation ADR). Continues [2026-05-22 C1–C2](decisions/2026-05-22-atlas-typed-promotion-access-utility.md). Log: [[log/2026-05-22-canonical-feature-ownership-c4]].

- [2026-05-21 Atlas Observe rail: pasture / conventional crop / berm / raised bed → Agricultural](decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-observe-rail-pasture-crops-earthworks-to-agricultural.md) — Observe-only left-rail re-grouping. EWE (Earth-Water-Ecology) is for ecological/observational facts — water, soil, vegetation cover. The four relocated tools describe how the land is **farmed or shaped for production**, so they belong with the productive buildings (barn, greenhouse, shed, animal shelter, compost station) already in the Agricultural rail section. Implementation extends the existing `BE_TOOL_GROUPS`-render `sourceItems` ternary in `ObserveTools.tsx` with a sibling `group.category === 'agricultural'` branch — mirrors the 2026-05-14 `amenity → terrace` precedent. Pasture and conventional-crop retain their EWE-prefixed toolIds (`observe.earth-water-ecology.pasture` / `conventional-crop`) via a per-kind `let toolId` switch in the downstream `groupItems` map, so their existing draw + store pipelines (`pastureStore`, `conventionalCropStore`) and EWE dashboard / `EcologicalDetail` surfacing are unchanged. Berm and raised-bed continue to dispatch BE toolIds unchanged. Rejected alternatives: (a) registry recategorisation (`earthworks → agricultural` in `builtEnvironmentKinds.ts`) — would regress Plan's 2026-05-14 placements of berm under `water-management` and raised-bed under `plant-systems`; (b) first-class `agriculture` Observe module — no checklist/store/dashboard exists, multi-slice cost with no current driver. Side-effects: Agricultural section-header click still routes to `built-environment` module (`BE_CATEGORY_TO_OBSERVE_MODULE.agricultural`), tool-button `stopPropagation` ensures pasture/conventional-crop activation doesn't force a module switch. Verified live at `/v3/project/mtc/observe` — EWE section now Watercourse/Soil sample/Vegetation & cover only; Agricultural section now adds Pasture/paddock, Conventional crop, Berm, Raised bed after the five productive buildings. Single-file change (commit `acf3009f`). Plan rail intentionally untouched.
- [2026-05-21 Atlas Vite dev proxy translates upstream failures into the API envelope](decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-vite-proxy-api-offline-envelope.md) — Closes the "Response not JSON (500)" papercut on `POST /api/v1/auth/register`. Symptom traced to Vite's dev proxy returning plain-text HTML when the API at `localhost:3001` was unreachable (`ECONNREFUSED`) — the API's own `setErrorHandler` always emits JSON, so a non-JSON 500 cannot originate there. Fix: added `configure` + `proxy.on('error', …)` to the `/api` proxy in `apps/web/vite.config.ts` that emits a `503` carrying the API's own envelope shape `{ data: null, error: { code: 'API_OFFLINE', message: "API server unreachable at http://localhost:3001 (<errno>). Start it with:  pnpm --filter @ogden/api dev" } }`. `apiClient.ts` flows through unchanged; LoginPage `role="alert"` banner now renders an actionable instruction instead of a misleading parser-error. Rejected alternatives: client-side fix (wrong seam — bakes dev-environment diagnosis into shipped code), retry/backoff (masks the operator's "API not started" mistake), block Vite-without-API (too coupling). Iteration note: first draft wrapped the command in backticks; PowerShell parsed those as line-continuation when an operator pasted the banner verbatim — plain-text form is copy-paste safe. Verified end-to-end (API down → 503 + envelope + banner DOM matches; API up → 201 + token). No edits to auth routes, no migrations, no seed-user script. Continues [2026-05-20 walkthrough](decisions/2026-05-20-olos-new-user-journey-walkthrough.md) gap closes.
- [2026-05-21 Atlas Phase D — J-curve + SOM trajectory + covenant rename](decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-phase-d-jcurve-and-som-trajectory.md) — Apricot-Lane Phase D closes the protocol's "Phase 3 — Feasibility / J-Curve + longitudinal SOM" gap with seven per-sub-phase commits on `feat/atlas-permaculture`: **D.1 (`31938a4c`)** new `apps/web/src/features/financial/engine/transitionBudget.ts` — pure aggregation `computeTransitionBudget(cashflow)` labels years `establishment 0-2` / `build-up 3-5` / `maturation 6+`, plus `jCurveTrough(years)` returning `{ troughYear, troughValue, breakevenYear }`; additive optional `Scenario.transitionBudgetMid?` + `Scenario.naturalCapitalAppreciationByYear?` on `scenarioStore`. **D.2 (`b5f69dd9`)** migration `031_som_trajectory_yearly` mirrors `succession_milestones` keyed on `(project_id, zone_id, year)` with `j_curve_stage` CHECK aligned to D.1's `TransitionPhase` vocabulary (`031` bumped from the originally-planned `029` because Three Streams Farm seeds took `029`+`030`). **D.3 (`13ee28e0`)** extends `apps/api/src/services/terrain/algorithms/soilRegeneration.ts` with `somPctToStockTcha` (Van Bemmelen × bulk-density × depth) + `projectSomTrajectory` (3-band scalar 0.25/0.6/1.0 applied to caller-supplied mature seqRate, year-by-year accumulation capped at target stock); new project-scoped route `/api/v1/soil-regeneration/project/:projectId/som-trajectory` (`GET` any role, `POST recompute` owner|designer) using DELETE-then-INSERT inside a transaction for the NULL `zone_id` UNIQUE quirk. **D.4 (`c77b96e5`)** new pure-SVG `apps/web/src/features/financial/JCurveChart.tsx` (recharts deliberately rejected — every existing in-app chart is pure SVG, simplifies the PDF embed) mounted on both the live `EconomicsPanel` (TanStack Query SOM fetch) and each captured scenario card in `ScenarioPanel`; D.1 scenarioStore producers go live here — `ScenarioPanel.handleCreate` becomes async, populates `transitionBudgetMid` synchronously via `computeTransitionBudget(model.cashflow)` and best-effort fetches `api.soilRegeneration.getSomTrajectory(projectId)` to derive `naturalCapitalAppreciationByYear` via new `somAppreciation.ts` helper (`USD_PER_TC_DEFAULT = 50` mid-range SCC proxy; D.7 may override). **D.5 (`e1364402`)** `scenarioComparison.ts` gains an "External Reference Profiles" section (Farmland LP + SLM Partners as informational public-disclosure benchmarks; framing: "External benchmarks shown for context; not a forecast and not a solicitation."); first half of the covenant rename pass — `'10-Year ROI'` → `'10-Year Operating Estimate'`, `'Highest Financial Return'` → `'Strongest Operating Estimate'`. **D.6 (`52d09091`, foreign-absorbed)** covenant rename in `capitalPartnerSummary.ts:117` (`'10-Year Project Yield'` → `'Operating Estimate at Maturity (Year 10)'`) + `CapitalPartnerSummaryExport.tsx:202` matching label — the staged D.6 strings were absorbed cleanly into a foreign WIP commit during a web-lint window (exactly the failure mode [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]] warns about); verified via grep that HEAD contains the new strings. **D.7 (`78627307`)** extends `FinancialPayload` with optional `jCurve { transitionYears, naturalCapitalAppreciationByYear?, troughYear, troughValue, breakevenYear, chartSvg? }`; web producer in `CapitalPartnerSummaryExport.handleGenerate` derives the payload via `computeTransitionBudget` + `jCurveTrough` + best-effort SOM trajectory fetch; server template gains a `renderJCurveSvg` helper producing a 480×220 inline SVG that mirrors `<JCurveChart>` — phase bands, dual y-axis labels, zero-line, trough + breakeven dashed markers, optional secondary dashed natural-capital line, primary path with dot markers — diverged from the plan's PNG-base64 sketch in favour of inline SVG to match D.4's pure-SVG house-style decision; - [2026-05-20 Atlas Phase C — Agent workforce + rotation→revenue bridge](decisions/2026-05-20-atlas-phase-c-agent-workforce-rotation-engine.md) — Apricot-Lane Phase C closes two protocol gaps with two commits on `feat/atlas-permaculture`. **C.6 (`8418062a`)** widens `ClaudeClient.callAnthropic` to accept a `string | SystemBlock[]` (string callers unchanged — wrapped into a single ephemeral-cached block exactly as before) and widens the return to `{ text, model, inputTokens, outputTokens }`; exports `SYSTEM_PROMPT`; adds public `chatWithRole({ roleSystemAddendum, userMessage })` that builds the canonical 2-block array — `[0]` cached Atlas base prompt with `cache_control: { type: 'ephemeral' }`, `[1]` role addendum. New `apps/api/src/services/ai/agentRegistry.ts` exports `AgentRole` (`'agro-designer' | 'hydro-engineer' | 'general'`), a static role-prompt table, pure `routeIntent(text)` (case-insensitive word-boundary keyword tally — hydro keywords: `swale`, `keyline`, `pond`, `water`, `hydro`, `runoff`, `infiltration`, `drainage`, `riparian`, `aquifer`, `cistern`, `dam`, `creek`, `flood`; agro keywords: `orchard`, `paddock`, `tree`, `plant`, `species`, `crop`, `pasture`, `grazing`, `livestock`, `rotation`, `cover crop`, `compost`, `silvopasture`; ties or zero → `'general'`), and `runAgent` which composes the addendum, calls `chatWithRole`, and parses any trailing `HANDOFF: <role> — <reason>` line (en-dash `—` or ASCII `--`) into `handoff: { to, reason } | null` (server **does not** auto-chain — caller decides). New route `POST /api/v1/ai/agent-chat` appended to `apps/api/src/routes/ai/index.ts` with `authenticate + resolveProjectRole` (project-membership; reads-only). 24-case test suite mirrors the `ClaudeClient.test.ts` global-`fetch`-stub pattern. **C.7 (`6a61d6cf`)** lands `apps/web/src/features/livestock/engine/rotationEngine.ts` (`computeRotationCalendar({ paddocks, herdSize, animalUnitMonths?, parasiteBreakDays = 60, grazeDaysPerPaddock = 3 })`) — wraps canonical `computeRotationCarryingCapacity` via a synthetic single-mob `RotationPlan` (every paddock in one cell group, `targetGrazeDays = grazeDaysPerPaddock`, `targetRestDays = parasiteBreakDays`) plus mob-grazed paddock list with per-paddock `stockingDensity = herdSize / areaHa` so the AU math is never forked; `cycleDays = grazeDaysPerPaddock × paddocks.length`, `recoveryDays = cycleDays − grazeDaysPerPaddock`, `annualAuDays = herdSize × 365`, `cyclesPerYear = floor(365 / cycleDays)`, `parasiteBreakCompliant = every entry's recoveryDays ≥ parasiteBreakDays`; degenerate input returns a well-formed zero calendar. New `apps/web/src/features/financial/engine/livestockRevenue.ts` (`buildLivestockRevenueStream(calendar, { pricePerAuDay, startYear = 1, maturityYear?, confidence = 'medium', assumptions?, id?, name? })`) — `annualRevenue.{low,mid,high} = pricePerAuDay.{...} × annualAuDays` (rounded); default 5-year build-up ramp `[0.2, 0.4, 0.65, 0.85, 1.0]` plateauing at 1.0 through year 10; `assumptions[]` surfaces herd × 365 AU-days, rotation cycle + paddock count, parasite-break compliance line (✓ "Parasite-break floor met (Xd minimum rest)" vs ✗ "WARNING: parasite-break floor NOT met — recovery Yd < Xd"), utilization + status; default `enterprise: 'livestock'`. The stream slots into `computeCashflow([], [stream], phases, horizon)` with **zero engine change** (cashflow consumer already iterates `stream.rampSchedule[y] × stream.annualRevenue.{...}`). `RotationScheduleCard.tsx` gains an additive "Cycle engine" summary block between the status pills row and per-group timelines: `cyclesPerYear`, `annualAuDays` (locale-formatted), parasite-break badge (green ≥ 60d / amber < 60d), utilization % with `ok` / `tight` / `over` status pill. Card uses an implied-mob 1 AU/ha heuristic (`Math.max(1, round(totalHa))`) clearly labelled in the header until herd-size capture lands — heuristic falls away by a one-line `useMemo` change, no engine signature change. Existing ad-hoc moves table untouched per [[feedback_no_deletion]]; plan-driven `RotationSequenceCard.tsx` left alone (engine decoupled from `RotationPlan`). 16 new tests (8 rotation-engine + 8 livestock-revenue) cover 11 × 3-day graze → `cycleDays 33` / `recoveryDays 30` / non-compliant; 11 × 6-day graze → `cycleDays 66` / `recoveryDays 60` / compliant; 50 AU × 365 = 18,250 AU-days; 200-acre fixture at 1 AU / 2 acres → 36,500 AU-days; degenerate empty + zero-herd paths; `annualRevenue.mid = pricePerAuDay.mid × annualAuDays`; enterprise tag; ramp 0 before startYear + monotone non-decreasing through plateau; startYear shift; WARNING / Parasite-break-floor-met assumptions; end-to-end `computeCashflow` integration (year-0 = 0, year-1 > 0, year-10 ≥ year-1). Gate: API tsc clean; `pnpm --filter @ogden/api run test` **653 passed / 3 skipped (656)** across 60 files; web tsc shows only the pre-existing `StepBoundary.tsx(365,7)` `unknown→ReactNode` foreign-WIP error (verified via stash-baseline comparison); `pnpm --filter @ogden/web run test` **1620 passed (1620)** across 157 files (incl. 24 C.6 + 16 C.7 new cases). Manual 200-acre fixture smoke deferred per Assumption A2. Covenant + IA: no CSRA / *bayʿ mā laysa ʿindak* / salam reintroduced; "capital partners & allies" preserved (livestock revenue is steward-facing operating estimate, not investor yield); 3-item Observe/Plan/Act IA unchanged; mobile Overview stack stays flat (engine block lands on the card, not the mobile shell).
