- [2026-05-20 Atlas Phase B — Design Map generator service](decisions/2026-05-20-atlas-phase-b-design-map-generator.md) — Apricot-Lane Phase B closes the core missing capability the protocol identified: a pure-function `generateDesignMap(input)` orchestrator under `apps/api/src/services/designMap/` that emits candidate `path` + `zone` `CreateDesignFeatureInput` rows from terrain + watershed baselines, no new map stack and no new dependency. Four algorithms, each in its own per-sub-phase commit: **B.2.orchard** (`orchardOnContour.ts` — contour-clipped `path / farm_lane` rows + spacing-based tree count, warns rather than fails when contours absent); **B.2.swale** (`keylineSwales.ts` — consumes `WatershedRefinementProcessor` candidate shape verbatim, `path / farm_lane / water` rows with `depth × width × fillFactor × length` sponge-capacity model, run **unconditionally** when candidates present because swales are infrastructure not enterprise); **B.2.paddock** (`paddockGrid.ts` — N×M bbox subdivision default 4×3, inward-buffer for fence alley, `zone / livestock / grazing` rows + `acres × auPerAcre × 365` AU-days, **gated on `enterprises.includes('livestock')`**); **B.2.corridor** (`habitatCorridors.ts` — perimeter donut polygon **always emitted** on a valid parcel + optional riparian strip from `LineString` inputs, `zone / conservation / habitat`; slope-aware spine deferred since `geometry.ts` lacks a centreline primitive). Scaffolding in **B.1** ships `DesignMapGenerator.ts` orchestrator + zero-dependency `geometry.ts` (local equirectangular projection anchored on parcel centroid latitude, haversine, polygon area/centroid, point-in-polygon, polyline offset, **bisector-scaled inward ring buffer** `d × (u1+u2)/(1+u1·u2)` so concave corners don't overshoot, bbox). **B.3** pins three cross-algorithm contracts: full-stack run on 900 m square + 3 contours + livestock yields orchards + paddocks + corridors together; `sortOrder` banding 100s/200s/300s/400s by algorithm; warning aggregation distinctness ("no contours" surfaces exactly once). **B.4** lands as a gate-of-record (no commit) — `pnpm --filter @ogden/api run lint` clean, `pnpm --filter @ogden/api run test` **624 passed / 3 skipped (58 files)** including the 66-case designMap suite (23 geometry + 7 orchard + 8 swale + 8 paddock + 7 corridor + 13 orchestrator). Riparian extraction from `drainage_divide` (polygons from `binaryMaskToGeoJSON`, not LineStrings) deferred — B.5.1 passes `undefined` and perimeter fallback satisfies the protocol's "candidate corridors" requirement. Six commits ahead of origin on `feat/atlas-permaculture` pending the B → B.5 boundary push: `776901fa` (B.1) → `89c233cf` (B.2.orchard) → `3d4cd9ff` (B.2.swale) → `90a8b4e0` (B.2.paddock) → `5e9c1956` (B.2.corridor) → `c190ac59` (B.3). Continues [2026-05-20 Phase A](decisions/2026-05-20-atlas-phase-a-apricot-lane-decision-layer.md); next is B.5 — Fastify route `POST /design-map/project/:projectId/generate` + web `apiClient` + dry-run `DesignMapGeneratorModal` + `DomainFloatingToolbar`/`NextBestActionsPanel` triggers.

- [2026-05-20 B3 — Rotation-sequence spine push (seed projected moves to WorkItems)](decisions/2026-05-20-atlas-b3-rotation-sequence-spine-push.md) — Closes the D-stage gap left by the B3 read-only sequencer: projected `MoveCalendarEntry[]` from `projectRotationSequence` now seeds a new `source: 'rotation-sequence'` WorkItem family with composite provenance `<cellGroup>__<paddockId>__<sequenceOrder>__<cycleIndex>`, `scheduledStart`/`scheduledEnd` mapped 1:1 from `computeMoveCalendar` projections, and `precedesAuto` chained linearly **within each cellGroup** (cross-cellGroup edges deliberately omitted — cellGroups graze independently). Mirrors the cover-crop spine-push template proven in `coverCropSpineSync.ts` 1:1. Schema additions (additive): `WorkItemSource` enum gains `'rotation-sequence'` (8th value); `WorkItem.generatedFromRotationMove?: string` provenance field adjacent to `generatedFromCoverCropWindow`; `syncManifest['ogden-work-items'].schemaVersion` 3→4 (additive enum + optional field, no migration). Two new store actions write the family: `replaceRotationSequenceRows(projectId, rows)` and `replaceRotationSequenceDependencies(projectId, depMap)` — both gated by `source === 'rotation-sequence' && !overridden`; cross-source preservation hard-locked (manual + goal-compass + overridden rows survive bitwise across either call; idempotent same-array short-circuit on dependencies). New orchestrator `pushRotationSequenceToSpine(projectId)` wired into four explicit call sites: `RotationSequenceCard` "Sync schedule" button (new, sibling of the Read-only badge); `OvergrazedEditor.save()` (shorten-move flow); `RestEditor.save()` (extend-rest flow); `UnplannedPaddockEditor.save()` (insert-one-off-move flow). **No auto-push** on `paddockStore`/`rotationPlanStore` mutations — push is always explicit or piggybacks an editor Save (prevents thrash on every paddock-name typo). Internal `withCycleIndex` helper counts prior occurrences of each `paddockId` per `cellGroup` to recover `cycleIndex` (`computeMoveCalendar` returns entries in cellGroup-then-cycle-then-cell order but doesn't emit the index). Internal `resolvePhaseId` mirrors cover-crop phase resolution (id match → name case-insensitive → `null`). Strictly-additive: no new `MODULE_CARDS` row (card already mounted at `plan-livestock-rotation-sequence`), no per-move `materialsAuto`/`costRangeAuto` (livestock moves carry no per-move agronomic inputs in the current data model — future slice if salt/mineral/water-haul kits become per-move concerns), no `LivestockMoveEvent` mutation (observe-stage immutable audit trail), no goal-tree criterion / readiness gating, no cross-cellGroup `precedesAuto` edges, no `WorkItem.overridden` UI. Covenant clean — strictly agronomic: copy "Rotation move"/"graze"/"rest"/"schedule"; no riba/gharar/CSRA/salam/investor/financing/cost-of-capital/payback/ROI vocabulary (covenant grep only matches negative-assertion guards in the spine-sync docstring + the editors covenant test). Gate: targeted vitest **14/14** (`rotationSequenceSpineSync.test.ts` — provenance format, seeder single-group/multi-cycle/multi-cellGroup/empty/phase-resolution/plan-defaults, dependency within-cellGroup chaining/no-cross-edges, orchestrator preservation gate + cross-source independence + idempotent re-push); full apps/web vitest **1562/1562** (was 1548; +14); `tsc --noEmit` pre-existing `precedesAuto` shape errors in `workItemStore.migration.ts` + `seedGoalCompass*` tests inherited from B5.2.x.c remain (no new errors reference the B3 surface); branch divergence `0/0` against `@{u}` before any push. - [2026-05-20 B5.2.x.c follow-up — Map-entry wire-up](decisions/2026-05-20-atlas-b5-2-x-c-cover-crop-spine-completion.md#addendum-2026-05-20--map-entry-wire-up-closed) — Closes the explicit deferred sub-item from the B5.2.x.c spine-completion ADR. New `PlanCropAreaSelectionHandler` (`apps/web/src/v3/plan/draw/PlanCropAreaSelectionHandler.tsx`, ~90 LOC, props `{ map, projectId }`) listens for `mousedown` on the Plan-stage MapLibre canvas, queries live `crop-fill-*` layers via `map.getStyle().layers` + `map.queryRenderedFeatures(e.point, { layers })`, resolves `cropAreaId` from `properties.id` → `properties.cropAreaId` → strip `crop-fill-` prefix off `top.layer.id` (the MapCanvas/CropPanel sources stamp only `{ name }` today, so the layer-id strip is the live path), and dispatches `useCoverCropPopoverStore.getState().openFor({ projectId, cropAreaId, anchor: { x: e.point.x, y: e.point.y } })` with `e.preventDefault()` + `e.originalEvent.stopPropagation()`. Screen-space anchor because the C6 popover ships hand-rolled fixed positioning, not map-coordinate. Mounted in `apps/web/src/v3/plan/PlanLayout.tsx` (append-only): handler adjacent to `<PlanObserveSelectionHandler map={map} />` line 205; `<CoverCropPopoverEditor />` adjacent to `<InlineFeaturePopover map={map} />` line 232. Left-click → direct popover (vs. right-click context-menu or select-then-chip) — matches `PlanObserveSelectionHandler`'s mousedown precedent and is the smallest surface. Strictly-additive: no new store (C6 already shipped `useCoverCropPopoverStore`), no schema bump, no `inlineFormStore` change, no impact on the other 23 map tools. Single-writer preserved: Save still funnels through `updateCropArea` + `pushCoverCropPlanToSpine`. Gate: targeted vitest **7/7** (4 new `PlanCropAreaSelectionHandler` cases — happy path with `properties.id`, fallback strip from layer-id, no-op when no `crop-fill-*` layer live, no-op when `projectId` null — plus existing 3-case `CoverCropPopoverEditor` suite); full apps/web vitest **1536/1536** (150 files); `apps/web` tsc exit 0; `packages/shared` tsc exit 0; covenant grep clean on the two new files. MapLibre canvas-click not exercised under harness (WebGL hang disclosure rule); vitest + tsc authoritative. - [2026-05-20 B5.2.x.c — Cover-crop spine completion (terminate-before edges + scheduled dates + map-entry popover + multi-area bulk apply)](decisions/2026-05-20-atlas-b5-2-x-c-cover-crop-spine-completion.md) — Closes the four explicit non-goals deferred by [[2026-05-20-atlas-b5-2-x-b-cover-crop-seed-cost-labor-rollup]]: (1) terminate-before-cash-crop prerequisite seeding via new denormalized inverse edge `WorkItem.precedesAuto: string[]` written only on cover-crop rows by new `replaceCoverCropDependencies` action (mirrors `replaceGoalCompassDependencies` 1:1, preservation gate hard-locked) and unioned by `packages/shared/src/lib/workItemGraph.ts:buildEffectiveGraph` via a new inverse pass (`dependsOn ∪ dependsOnAuto ∪ inverse(precedesAuto)`); chosen over mutating the cash-crop side's `dependsOnAuto` to preserve single-writer (any cover-crop write into a `source: 'goal-compass'` row would collide with `replaceGoalCompassDependencies` on next goal-compass regen); (2) scheduled-date seeding via new pure `inferCoverCropDates(window, projectStartYear)` — start clamped to day 01, end clamped to day 28 (safe for all months including Feb non-leap), wrap-aware year+1 when `endMonth < startMonth`, project start year resolved through `resolveProjectStartYear(LocalProject.startDate ?? null)` with `new Date().getFullYear()` fallback; (3) map-drawn editor entry via new `MonthBandPicker` (12-segment horizontal band, controlled props, internal start/end click toggle, wrap-aware aria-pressed highlight) + new `CoverCropPopoverEditor` (standalone screen-anchored fixed-position popover wrapping list + add-form + Save, single-writer Save funnels through `updateCropArea` + `pushCoverCropPlanToSpine`, carries its own `useCoverCropPopoverStore` zustand store with `{ open, projectId, cropAreaId, anchor?, openFor, close }`); (4) multi-area bulk apply on `CoverCropPlannerCard` via collapsible "Apply to other areas" chip multi-select (component-local `useState<Set<string>>`, not persisted), parent `onSave` loops `updateCropArea(otherId, { coverCropPlan: mergeWindows(existing, draft) })` per selected id and calls `pushCoverCropPlanToSpine(projectId)` exactly once — pure `mergeWindows` structural-dedup append (same speciesId+role+startMonth+endMonth ⇒ no duplicate) preserves existing plans on target areas. Forks ratified (verbatim AskUserQuestion): "All four in one B5.2.x.c" + orphan-cash-crop case = "Warn in the editor" (the spine writes no edge silently; the planner surfaces a banner above `AddWindowForm` *"No cash crop scheduled on this area yet — a terminate-before edge will be created when one is added"* resolved via `cashCropAreaIds` memo over `useWorkItemStore.items` filtered by `generatedFromPlantingCalendar` provenance `${species}:${cropAreaId}:${year}`). New pure `seedCoverCropDependencies({ coverCropItems, cashCropItems }): Map<itemId, string[]>` joins on shared `cropAreaId` parsed from the two provenance formats (`generatedFromCoverCropWindow` `${cropAreaId}__${idx}` vs `generatedFromPlantingCalendar` `${species}:${cropAreaId}:${year}`); orphan area emits empty array (B4/B5 omitted-not-stubbed). Schema delta: `WorkItem.precedesAuto: z.array(z.string()).default([])` (additive at the Zod layer via default-empty) + `syncManifest['ogden-work-items'].schemaVersion` 2→3 (records the field addition) — **not strictly-additive**, scoped exception pre-ratified by the "all four in one slice" answer. Single-writer preserved: only `replaceCoverCropDependencies` writes `precedesAuto`, and only on `source: 'cover-crop'` rows; cross-source mutation explicitly forbidden in test gates. **Explicit deferred follow-up:** the planned `CropAreaTool` map context-menu click-handler ("Edit cover crops" → `useCoverCropPopoverStore.openFor(...)`) is parked — `useInlineFormStore`'s field-spec API can't host the rich multi-window editor; the popover ships fully wired and callable programmatically, but the actual map-side `onSelectExistingFeature` ↔ popover-store binding awaits a larger design discussion (generalize `inlineFormStore` to host rich content vs. route per-feature-type into different popover stores). Today's entry surfaces: Plan slide-up `plant-systems` `CoverCropPlannerCard` (existing, with new orphan warning + bulk apply) and anyone holding the popover store. Covenant clean (`/\b(riba|gharar|csra|salam|investor|financing|cost-of-capital|yield|payback|investment|roi|return\s+on)\b/i` matches only docstring negative declarations + the two existing covenant-grep tests). - [2026-05-19 B5 — Beneficial-organism habitat audit](decisions/2026-05-19-atlas-b5-beneficial-organism-habitat.md) — Last strictly-additive B-series slice (B5.1 carries the deferred cover-crop dimension). Composite habitat-quality score = plant-richness (`min(40, distinctBeneficialSpecies * 4)`) + structural (`min(40, (hedgerowM/100 + pondM²/500 + shrubCount) * 4)`) + functional-diversity bonus (`min(20, distinctCategories * 5)`), clamped 0..100. Static cited `beneficialFunctionCatalog.ts` maps four PLANT_CATALOG `ecologicalFunction` tags + three `DesignKind` values onto seven `BeneficialCategory` buckets (Xerces / Cornell / UC IPM / NRCS / Audubon citations). `BeneficialHabitatCard` cross-registered into `habitat-allocation` + `plant-systems` (one sectionId, B4 precedent). New `beneficial-organism-habitat-pct` criterion (target 60 by Y3) sits as sibling of `regen-habitat-pct` under `biodiversity-habitat`. Beetle-bank / insectary-strip / bird-box / bat-box `DesignKind` values omitted-not-stubbed; A2/A3 cards untouched. 3 commits (`36b22ae2`/`bf9be395`/`d9f6f49d`), 30/30 targeted + 1358/1358 full vitest, tsc + vite build clean, covenant grep clean.

Sort comparator copied verbatim from D5 (`SEVERITY_RANK` → count desc → id asc). House date guard: malformed `now` → `Date.now()`. - [2026-05-19 D5 — operating dashboards & adaptive recommendations](decisions/2026-05-19-atlas-d5-operating-dashboards.md) — **The final ratified D slice — the D-series (D0–D5) is complete.** Pure composition engine `packages/shared/src/lib/operatingHealth.ts` (no React/store/I/O): `computeOperatingHealth(input)` consumes the *already-computed* results of the four D1–D4 engines (`analyzeWorkItemGraph`/`analyzeResourcing`/`analyzeBudget`/`analyzeFieldProof`) — it **composes, never re-derives** (budget drift stays D3-owned, surfaced verbatim, never re-framed toward financing/capital) — and returns four `Light` (`ok|warn|alert`) thresholds (schedule: alert if cyclic/critical-blocked, warn if overdue/blocked; resourcing: alert if equipment double-book, warn if over-capacity; budget: alert if drift ∧ total variance.mid > planned.high, warn if drift only; proof: alert if done-closure < 0.5, warn if any unproven) + seven deterministic ranked recommendations (cycle/blocked-critical/equipment-conflict = high, over-capacity/budget-drift/overdue = med, unproven = low; ranked severity→count desc→stable `id` tiebreak) + a `counts` block. Never reads/writes `WorkItem.status` (pinned by `Object.freeze` invariant test). Render-only card `apps/web/src/features/act/OperatingDashboardCard.tsx` (new): four store read-selectors + three D4 stores, runs the four engines in one `useMemo`, mirrors `BudgetCard`'s `{actual,actualHrs}` actuals map and `FieldProofPanel`'s five-store linkage + `domainEvents`(`windowDays:7`) derivation exactly so counts match the D3/D4 surfaces; three blocks (health lights + counts, recommended next actions, on-track empty state); deep-link targets are non-navigating labelled hints (no cross-card nav wired — YAGNI). Append-only `act-operating-dashboard` registration beside the `act-budget` anchor at the six mount points (`v3/act/types.ts`, `v3/act/ActModuleSlideUp.tsx`, `features/dashboard/DashboardRouter.tsx`, `features/act/ActHub.tsx`, `features/navigation/taxonomy.ts`, `components/stage-navigator/stageModules.ts`) — one additive hunk each, no reorder/mutation. **No store, no `syncManifest`, no schema, no DB migration.** Three resolved forks: deterministic rule-based (no ML/scoring model), fully render-only (no store/persistence; dismiss/snooze deferred YAGNI), new dedicated card. Covenant: strictly operating analytics — no riba/gharar/CSRA/salam, no cost-of-capital/financing/investor/yield-as-return framing; engine no-financing regex over `JSON.stringify` + card no-financing over rendered `textContent` + release-gate grep clean (only negative-assertion doc-comments match). Gate: shared+web tsc exit 0 clean; shared vitest **265/265 (19 files)** (operatingHealth 12 incl. no-status + no-financing invariants), web vitest **1233/1233 (117 files)** (OperatingDashboardCard 4); `vite build` exit 0 (`✓ built in 32.49s`, `--max-old-space-size=8192`); two-stage reviewed (spec ✅ + code-quality ✅ per task; final whole-implementation review APPROVED FOR BRANCH FINISH); MapLibre/WebGL live screenshot hang disclosed not faked (deep behind Act slide-up — tsc + suites authoritative). - [2026-05-19 B3.1 — rotational-grazing sequencer hardening (additive)](decisions/2026-05-19-atlas-b3-1-rotational-grazing-hardening.md) — Additive increment hardening sub-project B3 (which shipped fully out-of-band, `b790f85e..b36d5bf3` + ADR `cdf79c30`). Three template-mirrored parts, **no goal-tree criterion** (the B3 `livestock-rotation-rest-compliance-pct` criterion keeps reading `computeRestCompliancePct`, whose value simply becomes correct): (1) **honor `targetRestDays`** via private `honoredRestDays(cell, siblingGrazeSum) = max(siblingGrazeSum, cell.targetRestDays)` threaded through `computeMoveCalendar` (per-paddock idle-gap insertion when `cursor − lastMoveOut < honored`) and `computeRestCompliance` (`plannedRestDays = honored`) — the editable "Rest days" input is no longer a silent no-op; user-ratified as an *intentional correction* to B3's rendered numbers, not strictly behaviour-preserving (unlike B2.1) but **regression-safe by construction** because the 10 existing tests build cells via the `cell()` factory whose default is `targetRestDays:0` and `max(Σ-sibling-graze, 0) = Σ-sibling-graze`; (2) new pure `rotationCapacityMath.ts` — `computeRotationCarryingCapacity(paddocks, plan): GroupCapacityRow[]` per cell-group AU demand-days vs supply-days, `utilizationPct`, `cycleDays = max(Σ-graze, max_cell(grazeDays+targetRestDays))`, OK/Tight/Over status bands (<85/85–110/>110), AU-load **reusing** (not forking) `computePaddockRecommendedStocking` + `AU_FACTORS`, surfaced display-only in `RotationSequenceCard` beside the existing static overstock advisory; coarse heuristic, explicitly **not** a forage-budget model (B2.1 "not lab-grade" precedent); (3) **optional** plan fields `startDateISO?`/`horizonCycles?` on `RotationPlan` (persist `version:1` unchanged, **no `migrate`** — old rows tolerate `undefined`) + new `setPlanOptions` store action + `withOptions` carry-forward across `setPlan`/`upsertCell`/`removeCell`; `RotationPlanCard` toolbar `<input type="date">` + 1/2/3-cycle `<select>` (auto-persist, reuses existing `.field` class — no CSS change); `RotationSequenceCard` reads `plan.startDateISO ?? today` and `plan.horizonCycles ?? 1`. Strictly additive, non-covenant ("capacity" = animal-unit grazing load, never financial return — no riba/gharar/CSRA/salam/investor/financing/cost-of-capital/yield-as-return framing; covenant `not.toMatch` in `rotationCapacityMath.test.ts`). A-series additive covenant held: no DB migration/API/schema/goal-tree criterion/`Record<PlanModule,_>`/`syncManifest`/spine change; no registration change (cards already mounted under the `livestock` Plan slide-up). Cards keep the livestock-module house style (`features/livestock/`, `{ projectId }` prop) — B3's own convention, not the v3/plan `stageCard` path. Gate: web tsc 0 B3.1 errors over the six touched files (only pre-existing out-of-band D0 errors remain), shared tsc exit 0, vitest `rotationSequenceMath` 15 (10 pre-B3.1 unchanged + 5 new incl. explicit `targetRestDays:0 ⇒ identical to pre-B3.1` regression lock) + `rotationCapacityMath` 11 + `rotationPlanStore` 10 (6 prior + 4 new) — 36/36 green; full web suite **1282/1282** (121 files; consistent with B3.1 adds + the out-of-band `254ab499 feat(livestock): B3 plan-vs-actual rotation adherence` slice that landed between Parts 1 and 2, touches different files, outside scope); `vite build` exit 0; additive-isolation audit PASS — per-commit `git diff-tree` confirms each commit touches only its planned files. - [2026-05-17 Register custom 404/error handlers before route plugins](decisions/2026-05-17-atlas-error-handler-ordering.md) — `setNotFoundHandler`/`setErrorHandler` were registered *after* all route plugins, so Fastify served route contexts with its **default** handler: status codes stayed correct (`AppError.statusCode` honored) but the body shape was wrong (default `{statusCode,error,message}` instead of the app envelope `{data:null,error:{code,message}}`), and non-`AppError`/non-`ZodError` failures never got the `INTERNAL_ERROR` envelope. Moved both blocks **before** the route registrations (after `app.decorate('pipeline')`); handler bodies byte-for-byte unchanged. Latent/pre-existing — out of scope for the branch's defect fixes but corrected for consistent enveloping. Telemetry still returns 422 for validation failures (`ValidationError` is an `AppError`; status honored by both handlers — only the envelope changed). `@ogden/api` typecheck exit 0; **no test regressions** — the 11 build-app integration fails are pre-existing DB-environment breakage in a fresh worktree (no test DB), identical (9/11 on `smoke`+`telemetry`+`boundary`) with this change stashed. Landed in commit `6ac716b4`. **Correction (same day):** the "11 fails need a test DB" claim was wrong — see the lazy-thenable ADR below; the suite is mock-DB and all 11 were harness deficiencies, now 550/550.
- [2026-05-17 Mock DB harness: lazy-thenable upgrade](decisions/2026-05-17-atlas-mock-db-lazy-thenable.md) — Retires the false "11 `@ogden/api` tests need a provisioned database" premise. Suite is mock-DB by design (`vitest.config.ts` dummy `DATABASE_URL` + `vi.mock` FIFO queue). The 11 were harness deficiencies. Core fix: `testApp.ts` mock made a **lazy thenable** (shifts the queue only when awaited, memoized) mirroring real `postgres` `PendingQuery` — non-awaited interpolated SQL fragments no longer drain the queue (fixed telemetry-aggregate + comments). Added `mockDb.json`/`mockDb.begin`. Per-file drift fixed: `smoke` per-test `clear`, `boundary` missing `refuseIfBuiltin` row, `telemetry` 400→422 envelope, `siteAssessments` missing derived-layers `{present}` guard (the `maybe*` path is **8** awaited queries, not 7). One regression (`comments` placeholder enqueue that only fed the old eager bug) fixed at the test. `@ogden/api` typecheck exit 0; **550/550** (50 files), zero previously-passing tests flipped. Real-DB/testcontainers harness explicitly deferred.

- [2026-05-17 Full `syncService` coverage — Phase 4 (hydration + version-skew + visible conflict)](decisions/2026-05-17-atlas-syncservice-coverage-phase4.md) — Closes P0-1's **read half** (Phase 2 was push-only shadow). `applyForProject` added to all 62 `versioned-blob` descriptors via a `BlobShape {select,apply}` — project-isolated inverse of `select` (`store.setState((st)=>patch)`, other projects untouched). `hydrateProjectStateBlobs` called from `initialSync` step-4 loop **inside `isSyncing=true`** (applies don't re-enqueue), adopts server `rev` as next `baseRev`, clears `temporal()` undo post-hydrate. - [2026-05-17 Full `syncService` coverage — Phase 1 registry + Phase 2 generic versioned-blob transport](decisions/2026-05-17-atlas-syncservice-coverage-phase1-2.md) — The **durable P0-1 fix** the 2026-05-16 bundle-escape-hatch ADR deferred. **Phase 1:** `lib/syncManifest.ts` is the single source of truth — every project-scoped `ogden-` persist store is classified `typed-design-feature` (already on `design_features`; blob path forbidden — no double-write) / `typed-table` (veg/succession, Phase 3) / `versioned-blob` (the ~62 write-mostly remainder); a Vitest coverage guard scans store source for the persist `name:` and **fails the build** if any store is unclassified — the enumeration gap that *was* P0-1 is now un-regressable. **Phase 2 (push-only shadow, default-off `FLAGS.SYNC_STATE_BLOBS`):** migration `027_project_state_blobs.sql` (`PK(project_id,store_key)`, monotonic `rev`, `schema_version`); Fastify `routes/project-state/` (stale write sent as explicit `reply.code(409){serverRev,serverPayload}` — *not thrown*, because Fastify's default serializer drops `details`); shared `projectState.schema.ts`; client `blobSync.ts` (`409` duck-typed on `err.status`, module mocks split `ApiError` identity) + `'state-blob'` queue type + `executeStateBlobOp`. **P2.5b** (user: "full 62-store manifest now"): all 62 `versioned-blob` descriptors carry a live store handle + `scope` (`active-singleton`/`byProject`/`projectId-tagged`) + `schemaVersion` + `usesTemporal` + total `selectForProject` (helpers `whole`/`byKey`/`tagged`/`taggedFind` + bespoke `agribusinessSelect`); generic per-store ~800 ms-debounced `isSyncing`-guarded subscription loop in `syncService.start()`; in-memory `blobBaseRev` prevents rev-0 → permanent-409 lockout; on 409 the client adopts `serverRev` and logs (local slice **not** silently clobbered — visible reconcile is Phase 4). TDD RED→GREEN; diagnosed a Vitest artifact (`vi.mock`+`importActual`+wrapper double-tracks a *caught* rejection → use `vi.spyOn`; persist-store imports need `happy-dom`). `tsc` web exit 0; web **973/973** (no regression from 62-store import), shared 7/7, api projectState 4/4 incl. 409-staleness. Deferred: Phase 3 typed tables, Phase 4 hydration/version-skew/visible-conflict surface, Phase 5 phased enable + multi-device matrix; `projectBundle.ts` stays the offline backup until Phase 5.
- [2026-05-16 Multi-device project-bundle escape hatch + the partial-sync boundary](decisions/2026-05-16-atlas-multi-device-bundle-escape-hatch.md) — Pre-live-testing P0: `syncService` is fully implemented/auth-wired (the "orphaned" agent claim was a verified error) but syncs only **4 slices** (projects/zones/structures/comments) — the other ~66 `ogden-` persisted stores are localStorage-only *even authenticated*, so a multi-device tester silently loses the entire v3 design surface (design elements/vegetation/all Observe annotations/regen plans/metadata) with no warning. Full `syncService` coverage is the real fix but too large to gate testing on (deferred to backlog). Shipped instead: dependency-free `lib/projectBundle.ts` snapshots the **whole `ogden-` namespace** as opaque persist envelopes (prefix-capture is inherently complete — cannot miss a store; 4-key denylist for auth-token/matrix-toggles/connectivity/exported-flag), restore = remove-portable + overwrite + reload (stores re-hydrate + run own `migrate`); `parseBundle` defensively drops non-portable/non-string so a hand-edited bundle can't smuggle the auth token. `ProjectBundleBar` (mounted in `V3ProjectLayout`, rides every v3 route) is both the export/import entry point **and** the data-safety banner (prominent "lives in this browser" warning until first export via `hasExportedBundle()`, then collapses; import has an explicit "replace ALL + reload, cannot undo" confirm — a bundle is opaque so no per-field diff). 8/8 round-trip specs. Corrected stale `concepts/local-first-architecture.md`. No new npm deps.
- [2026-05-16 Auto-design paddock containment: steward opt-in + parcel clip + equal-area](decisions/2026-05-16-atlas-paddock-livestock-containment.md) — Fixes the steward report that **Generate site design** stamped paddocks outside the area drawn/deemed suitable for livestock ("the only consideration currently is the zone"). Three code-verified compounding defects: `permacultureZone` silently dropped at the call site (the existing `permacultureRingRange` hard-veto was dead production code); the allocator hard-vetoed only `avoidedCategories` so paddocks spilled into any `0`-scored zone once the livestock zone filled; and no parcel/suitability containment existed anywhere — amplified by `ringSeedGenerator` seeding a giant non-parcel-clipped Z4 `livestock` annulus that won the area tiebreak. Steward-confirmed: "Suitable for livestock" is an explicit per-zone **opt-in toggle** (not category/ring/draw-tool derived), containment is **strict + parcel-clipped**, and paddocks are roughly equal size (`(max−min)/max ≤ 0.10`). Fix (pure-engine first): optional `suitableForLivestock?` on `LandZone`/`AllocatorZone` (no `ogden-zones` persist bump); a strict `scoreZone` veto (`preferredCategories⊇livestock && suitableForLivestock !== true → return null`, the existing hard-veto contract → no spill, non-livestock unaffected) — so the unflagged Z4 ring gets zero paddocks and the amplifier collapses by construction; the call site maps `permacultureZone`+flag+`parcelBoundary` in; `runAutoDesign` clips `zone ∩ parcel` **before** subdivision for `tile-strip` only (reusing `parcelPolygon`/`intersectPolys`); `stripSubdivide` rewritten to bisect the sweep coordinate (28 iters, pure/no-RNG) until cumulative clipped area hits `k/n` of true area so equal-area holds on irregular polygons. `tsc --noEmit` exit 0; vitest **892/892** against the real unmocked pipeline (strict-veto + `zone ∩ parcel` containment + per-group `≤0.10` + zero-drafts-outside-parcel + determinism). One initial test failure was a **wrong assumption, not a bug** — `makeGoalTree()` selects `silvopasture-alley`+`integrated-stock-cropland` (not `cattle-/small-ruminant-` paddocks); the engine was provably correct (zone area exactly halved by the parcel clip, all strips equal, all within parcel), so the test's helper was re-keyed to the `tile-strip` template (the plan's actual contract). Live screenshot walkthrough unobtainable (WebGL/MapLibre returns black frames offline + deep stateful flow) — disclosed not faked; integration tests assert the steward's invariants with numeric precision. Deferred: parcel-clip for `edge-line` fences + `centroid/fill/bbox` regeneration-fill. Refines `2026-05-14-auto-design-pipeline.md`; interacts with the 2026-05-15 ring-seeder ADR (the amplifier).
- [2026-05-16 7-stage lifecycle is being retired — 3-item nav is the forward IA](decisions/2026-05-16-atlas-7-stage-lifecycle-retirement.md) — A `/graphify update` re-extraction (graph 2,867→7,642 nodes) surfaced as its top surprising connection that `3-item nav does not match 7-stage lifecycle` (docs/ux-walkthrough-regen-farm.md) is `semantically_similar_to` the [Atlas Sidebar — Permaculture-Grounded IA](concepts/atlas-sidebar-permaculture.md) concept, framed as an unresolved IA tension. Yousef resolved it directly: the **seven-stage lifecycle** (Discover/Observe → Diagnose → Design → Prove/Test → Build → Operate/Steward → Report/Evaluate) is **deprecated**; the 3-item nav is the forward-looking IA and is **not** to be conformed back to the seven stages. The sidebar concept page is retained as history (no-delete rule) but its active-spec recommendations are superseded for forward work; the Permaculture-Scholar rationale stays a valid input. Consequences: 7-stage refs in code/docs/wiki are legacy artifacts pending cleanup, not a spec to satisfy; graphify `query`/`surprising-connections` will keep returning 7-stage nodes until the source docs are retired/annotated; the formal cut (route slugs, `LIFECYCLE_STAGES`, sidebar component) is a future session — this ADR records the direction so intervening work does not invest in the deprecated model.
- [2026-05-16 Recompute acreage when a parcel boundary is drawn inside v3 Land OS](decisions/2026-05-16-atlas-v3-in-canvas-acreage-recompute.md) — Closes the deferred follow-up from the wizard→v3 bridge ADR. The three v3 boundary-persist handlers (PlanLayout/ActLayout `handleBoundaryDrawn`, ObserveLayout inline `onBoundaryDrawn`) persisted `parcelBoundaryGeojson` but **omitted `acreage`**; the adapter reads `LocalProject.acreage` straight (`p.acreage ?? 0`, never derives from polygon), so a parcel drawn *inside* Land OS left Report at "0 ha" (the wizard path already computed it). **Fix (helper + 3 handlers + wizard):** new `lib/geo.ts` `parcelAcreage(geo, units)` — verbatim relocation of the wizard's `turf.area`→`÷10000` (ha)/`÷4046.86` (ac), 2-dp, `try/catch→null`; arg union covers raw `Polygon` (handlers) + `FeatureCollection` (wizard). Each handler now sends `acreage: parcelAcreage(polygon, units)` (Observe added a `units` store selector, no `LocalProject` in scope); the wizard's inline block collapses to one call (now-unused `turf` import dropped) so all four call sites share one source of truth and can't drift. Persist (not adapter-derive) so non-v3 consumers (financial/AI/dashboards/syncService) stay consistent. `tsc --noEmit` exit 0. Verified offline via real Vite modules→store→adapter→ReportPage: ha 3.99/ac 9.87 (not inverted), live Report "US · 3.99 ha" / "US · 9.87 ac" (no "0 ha"); MTC sentinel unaffected (builtin key-filter drops `acreage`); re-draw updates not appends (single feature, 3.99→99.82). Out of scope: legacy `MapView` always-hectares bug (untouched, not deleted). Report route has no map canvas — DOM-text asserts, screenshot limitation N/A here.
- [2026-05-17 Backend acreage integrity (Full hardening): FeatureCollection→PostGIS + applyServerAcreage clobber guard](decisions/2026-05-17-atlas-backend-acreage-hardening.md) — Closes the *online* hole the P0 integrity guard explicitly deferred. Two root causes: (1) `POST /projects/:id/boundary` + template-instantiate passed the client's raw GeoJSON **FeatureCollection** to PostGIS `ST_GeomFromGeoJSON` (accepts only a bare Geometry) → NULL → `ST_Area(NULL)` → server `acreage 0`; (2) `applyServerAcreage` only rejected non-finite values — **accepted `0`** — clobbering the canonical client geodesic acreage. User scope: **Full hardening**. Fix: new pure shared `geojsonGeometry.ts` `extractPolygonalGeometry` (no turf — walks FC/Feature/GeometryCollection, merges polygons→MultiPolygon, `null` on nothing; never throws), exported from `index.ts`; `project.schema.ts` `parcelBoundaryGeojson` tightened from `z.unknown()` to a shape-only GeoJSON union; both backend call sites normalize before SQL — boundary route 4xx, template path skips the UPDATE (NULL self-heals) — **never write acreage 0**; `applyServerAcreage` guard now `<= 0`, exported for test. Verified: shared 201 tests (incl. 9 new) + tsc clean; api tsc clean + pre-DB rejection passes (the 11 build-app integration fails are pre-existing mock-db breakage from the co-landed blob-sync work, present on baseline with my changes stashed); web syncService 12/12 (incl. 3 guard cases). One remaining web tsc error `syncService.ts:765 'd.store' undefined` is inside the co-landed blob-sync `SYNCED_STORES` loop (outside the acreage guard — confirmed by stash), flagged to its owner not fixed here. Landed in `ddb7e0e4` (branch rebased out-of-band, folded with blob-sync).
- [2026-05-16 Parcel-area integrity guard + Water-balance honesty (no confident zeros)](decisions/2026-05-16-atlas-parcel-integrity-guard.md) — Builds on the in-canvas acreage-recompute ADR: that one makes a *drawn* boundary persist real acreage; this governs when acreage is *still* missing/zero. Run-2 walkthrough (#77/#78) found a naive user shown "ON, CA · 0 ha · Supported · 67/100 · 0 blocking issues". Two independent root causes: (1) `adaptLocalProject.ts` silently `null→0`, hardcoded `blockers:[]`, and let the verdict fall through to "Supported" on an unknown area; (2) **separate** — Water's `catchmentYieldM3` reads each node's manual `areaM2`, unset → silent `0 m³` collapsing the balance (the walkthrough's "0-ha is the root of Water" premise was wrong, surfaced honestly). User-approved scope: include Water + **hard-degrade** the verdict. Fix: new single-decision module `v3/data/parcelIntegrity.ts` (`isParcelAreaValid`, `formatLocationArea`, explicit `INTEGRITY_BLOCKER`/`INSUFFICIENT_DATA_VERDICT` deliberately **not** routed through `adaptVerdict`/`VERDICT_TABLE` so future scoring edits can't soften it); `adaptLocalProject.ts` is the sole guard seam (scorer input line left unchanged — verdict override supersedes); `ProjectLocation.areaKnown?` (optional → no fixture/`mtc` break); 5 display surfaces share `formatLocationArea`. Offline DOM-text verified (screenshot timed out on WebGL canvas — disclosed): Case A null/Case B 0 → "Area not set" + blocked verdict + 1 blocker; Case C valid 12 ha byte-for-byte unchanged ("49 Conditional", 0 blockers); Water zero-area → "incomplete" not 0, defaults + ground parcel-button gating, all-valid regression real "82.6 kL". Out of scope: backend `ST_GeomFromGeoJSON(FeatureCollection)`→0 + `applyServerAcreage` overwrite (online-only, deferred).

- [2026-05-15 Map cursor: `useMapCursor` is authoritative](decisions/2026-05-15-atlas-map-cursor-authoritative.md) — Fixes "cursor never changes / flashes then reverts to open hand while drawing". Two defects in the shared `useMapCursor.ts`: (1) hover probed only in `select` mode, so `pan` could never yield `pointer` — clickable affordance dead by construction everywhere; (2) the hook only re-applied its `cursor:…!important` on map `mousemove`, but mapbox-gl-draw + the Observe draw/drag tools write `canvas.style.cursor = ''` on click/dblclick/mouseup/keydown/cleanup (no following mousemove), stripping `!important` so the canvas inherits container `grab` and stays stuck. Fix: probe hover in pan too; add a `MutationObserver` on the canvas `style` attribute that re-asserts the computed cursor after any external clobber (equality guard → no feedback loop, disconnected on cleanup). ~30 ad-hoc `getCanvas().style.cursor` writers now redundant — left in place, removal deferred. typecheck exit 0; preview-verified on Observe (pan `grab`→arm draw `crosshair`→clobber→observer restores `crosshair` ~80 ms).

- [2026-05-13 Atlas Adopt-from-map v2 (basemap-hide + projectId fix)](decisions/2026-05-13-atlas-adopt-from-map.md) — Closes the user-perceived "Save does nothing" symptom on Observe's "Adopt from map" tool. Two bugs: (1) v1 adopt flow created the BE entity but the basemap kept rendering its own building extrusion underneath, producing z-fight; fixed by new `ExistingMetadata.adoptedFromBasemapId` field capturing the basemap tile's `osm_id` at click time, plus new `apps/web/src/features/map/adoptedBasemapBuildings.ts` which splices a property-based `['!', ['in', ['get', 'osm_id'], ['literal', ids]]]` filter clause onto every basemap building layer (preserving the layer's pre-adoption baseline filter in a per-map `WeakMap` cache, idempotent on every `style.load` + store change). Mounted via new `AdoptedBuildingsSync` component in v3 `ObserveLayout` + `VisionLayoutCanvas`, plus a direct `useEffect` in legacy `MapCanvas`. An earlier v2.1 attempt that injected `promoteId` via `removeSource`+`addSource` was rejected — MapLibre throws when layers reference the source, leaving the basemap destroyed mid-flight. (2) Sample-project route — `ObserveLayout` was the only v3 layout missing the `params.projectId ?? 'mtc'` fallback that `PlanLayout`/`ActLayout`/30 BE dashboards share; raw `undefined` threaded to `ObserveDrawHost`→`AdoptBasemapBuildingTool` triggered the early-return guard so the entity was never even created. Added `const id = params.projectId ?? 'mtc'` and swapped every store-aware child (`MapToolbar`, `DesignToolRail`, `ObserveAnnotationLayers`, the BE-layer block now mounted unconditionally, `ObserveDrawHost`, `AnnotationSectorHandles`, `SelectionFloater`, `ExportButton`, `ImportSiteIntelButton`, `AnnotationDetailPanel`) onto `id`. Auxiliary: `DesignElementExtrusionLayer` now prefers entity `proposed.heightM` and gains click-to-inline-edit (extrusion intercepts clicks before the 2D fill at pitched cameras); `elementHeights.ts` registers `building` as `mode: 'extrusion'` with 6 m single-storey fallback.

- [2026-05-12 Observe `--olos-*` tokens unified onto atlas palette](decisions/2026-05-12-atlas-observe-token-unification.md) — Follow-up to the same-day observe-port retirement. The 16 co-located Observe `.module.css` files still referenced the `--olos-*` namespace (49 occurrences, 10 distinct tokens); those declarations only ever existed in the deleted generated stylesheet plus the unimported sibling `apps/atlas-ui/src/styles.css`, so references with fallbacks rendered flat and references without (e.g. `--olos-green`, `--olos-font-display`, `--olos-panel`, `--olos-focus-ring`) silently dropped the property. No `.tsx` edits. Pre-flight grep zero hits in `apps/web/src/`; typecheck clean; preview-verified on Topography slide-up + charts. One token namespace now spans Observe / Plan / Act.

Broiler-Product-Map / agribusiness layer logged as deferred. Supersedes the 2026-05-08 Plan Module 4 Livestock ADR.
- [2026-05-10 Observe always-inert CTA audit](decisions/2026-05-10-atlas-observe-inert-cta-audit.md) — Single rule across v3 stages: if a CTA has no live target, delete it. 11 always-inert buttons removed across 10 Observe files (5 dashboards + 6 detail pages); Plan and Act stages were already clean. Decorative interactivity is an anti-pattern; wiring would require inventing targets (no action-plan generator, no export pipeline, no overlay route); deletion matches precedent from commit `4105ba4`. The `Create transect` button was the only one with a real backing surface (tools-panel draw tool one click away), so option A (delete uniformly) shipped over option B (wire-just-this-one). Unused `ArrowRight`/`Plus` imports dropped from 4 files.

- [2026-05-10 Act Livestock module — LivestockMoveCard (unified two-kind log)](decisions/2026-05-10-atlas-act-livestock-move-card.md) — Closes the third and last deferred Phase-3 follow-up: structure-anchored livestock-move events (from `ActStructurePopover.actions.startLivestockMoveLog` on barn / animal_shelter) wrote successfully to `useLivestockMoveLogStore` but had no read surface — `eventsByPaddock()` is paddockId-keyed and silently dropped `structureId`-only events. (Note: the ADR shipped with a framing error claiming paddock-anchored events were also invisible — `RotationScheduleCard` already rendered them inline per row. See the ADR's *Corrections* section.) The card adds three things: a read surface for structure-anchored events, a self-service write form (rotation card is read-only), and a unified at-a-glance log across both source kinds. Mirrors `MaintenanceLogCard`'s mixed-source-kind shape (one card, two label resolvers, kind-selector form) rather than the harvest split, because move events are shape-symmetric across both kinds. Mounted as second tab on the Livestock module between *Yield log* and *Rotation schedule*.
- [2026-05-10 LivestockMoveEvent v3 (from/to) + rotation-card rest variance](decisions/2026-05-10-atlas-livestock-move-event-v3.md) — Closes Gaps A and C from the LivestockMoveCard post-merge audit. Extends `LivestockMoveEvent` with `fromPaddockId` / `fromStructureId` / `toPaddockId` / `toStructureId` (legacy `paddockId` / `structureId` kept `@deprecated` for read-path fallback); persist v2→v3 migrate backfills `to*` from legacy fields. `RotationScheduleCard` now merges per-paddock entries with exits (deduped by id; handles `rotate_through`) and adds a *Structure moves* tail section listing all structure-destination events. Gap C ships plan-vs-actual rest variance: an `M of N entries on schedule · avg +Xd vs target` one-line summary per paddock + color-coded per-entry pills (green `+Nd rest` / neutral `on time` / amber `−1d`/`−2d` / red `−Nd` at ≥3 under). Pragmatic deviation from approved plan: popover + draw-tool inline forms did **not** gain a From picker (cramped floating panels); schema migration + in-card-form give full coverage and the From picker on those inline forms is a deferred follow-up. Gap B (inline write on rotation rows) closed same day in commit `4fca1b3` — each row gained a `+ Log move` button + compact in-row form. Pre-Gap-A cleanups bundled: S2 lifts canonical `DIRECTION_OPTIONS` / `SPECIES_OPTIONS` to the store (consumed by `LivestockMoveCard` and `ActStructurePopover.actions`; `LivestockMoveTool` still has inline copies — recorded as deferred); S3 adds a shared `.hint` class on `actCard.module.css` and backports per-kind empty-list hints to `MaintenanceLogCard`. Six commits: `5e3f1c4` (S2 + S3), `302f00b` (A2 schema + rotation card), `306e182` (Gap C retrospective variance), `4fca1b3` (Gap B inline log), `e248105` (S2 third-site cleanup — `LivestockMoveTool` imports canonical OPTIONS), `12d72b6` (forward-looking variance — new `scheduledLivestockMoveStore`, `Schedule…` per-row button, `Planned: <date>` line with variance pill, ±7d auto-fulfilment).

- [2026-05-04 P4 Public Portal — Section 27 Consolidation onto portal/*](decisions/2026-05-04-p4-public-portal-section27-consolidation.md) — Section 27's stub route + page were dead duplication of the working `portal/*` stack (share_token + `is_published` + `PortalRecord` schema + `PublicPortalShell.tsx`, all live since migration 004 in April). Stub deleted; cache + rate-limit gaps documented as TODO in `portal/public.ts` for the launch-readiness sprint. Closes 8.3-A.

Type-check green.
- [2026-05-07 Atlas Observe · Site Intelligence JSON Template Import](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-observe-site-intel-import.md) — New Import floater on the Observe map (above `ExportButton`) lets stewards download a JSON template scoped to the active project, fill it offline, and upload back to populate Tier-1 site intelligence. Single-source-of-truth template builder derives fillable fields from `LayerSummaryMap` and emits inline `__hint_*` siblings for offline guidance; Zod-strict top-level schema with `superRefine` enforcing `attribution` + `dataDate` when `include=true`. Per-layer override merge tags imports as `sourceApi: 'user_import'`, drops `enrichment`, and re-fires `enrichProject`. `isBuiltin` projects show the button disabled with "Read-only sample project." Validates: malformed JSON, missing required fields on `include=true`, projectId mismatch (warning only).
- [2026-05-07 Atlas Plan · Module 8 Three-Ethics rollup](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-plan-principles-three-ethics-rollup.md) — First follow-up landed from the Module 8 KEEP_ATLAS verdict. New `PERMACULTURE_ETHICS` constant maps each Holmgren principle to a single primary ethic (Earth Care: 5 principles; People Care: 4; Fair Share: 3). New sub-tab `plan-three-ethics-rollup` shows three ethic sections with constituent-principle status pills + per-ethic running tally + a `(met + 0.5×partial) / total` health pill (Met ≥70 % / Partial ≥30 % / Unmet). Reads existing `principleCheckStore` data — no persistence change. Mission-Statement cross-check + missing-principle radar/heatmap still deferred.
- [2026-05-07 Atlas Plan · Module 7 Scale-of-Permanence enhancement](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-plan-phasing-scale-of-permanence-enhancement.md) — First follow-up landed from the Module 7 KEEP_ATLAS verdict. Optional `designLayer?: 'earthworks' | 'water' | 'vegetation' | 'structures'` field added to `PhaseTask` (no persistence-version bump); `SeasonalTaskCard` exposes a Scale-of-permanence dropdown; new sub-tab `plan-phasing-scale-matrix` shows a fourth pivot view (Yeomans Keyline rows × phase columns) with sequencing-violation warnings when later layers (Structures/Vegetation) appear in a phase whose Earthworks/Water prerequisites are empty. Capacity-validation + cumulative-rollup follow-ups remain deferred.
- [2026-05-07 Atlas Plan · 8-Module Scholar Iteration (index ADR)](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-plan-modules-scholar-iteration.md) — Index + retrospective for the 8 per-module ADRs filed 2026-05-07. Tally: 5 BUILD_FRESH (3 additive, 2 net-new) + 3 KEEP_ATLAS + 0 PORT_OGDEN. Patterns: Atlas data models held up across the board (additive builds reuse existing stores); Scholar consistently rejected algorithmic verification where contextual reflection is the orthodox mechanic; OGDEN's strongest contributions were visual richness in Plants/Water; Yeomans Keyline appears in 3 modules with different meanings (rank ladder / chronological sequencing / explicitly rejected as retrospective rubric). Aggregates the deferred follow-ups across all 8 ADRs.
- [2026-05-07 Atlas Plan · Module 8 (Principle Verification) — KEEP_ATLAS](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-plan-principles-scholar-keep-atlas.md) — Eighth and final module of the 8-step Permaculture Scholar adjudication. Scholar ruled Atlas's `HolmgrenChecklistCard` (~187L: 12-principle rubric + free-text justification + 3-state status + linked-feature multi-pick across zone/path/structure/transect/guild/earthwork stores) "already architecturally aligned with orthodox permaculture pedagogy." Holmgren's 12 is the OSU PDC standard; the mechanic mirrors the PDC final-portfolio template (Application / Further Applied / Lessons Learned). Automated cross-checks explicitly rejected ("run counter to the contextual, observation-heavy nature of permaculture"); Yeomans Keyline Scales explicitly out of scope (sequencing tool, not retrospective rubric). OGDEN ships only a stub. Verdict KEEP_ATLAS, no code change. Three enhancements logged as follow-ups: (1) three-Ethics rollup (Earth Care / People Care / Fair Share); (2) Mission Statement / goals cross-check at the top; (3) missing-principle warnings + feature-type coverage matrix.
- [2026-05-07 Atlas Plan · Module 7 (Phasing & Budgeting) — KEEP_ATLAS](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-plan-phasing-scholar-keep-atlas.md) — Seventh module of the 8-step Permaculture Scholar adjudication. Scholar ruled Atlas's three-card phasing module (`PhasingMatrixCard` + `SeasonalTaskCard` + `LaborBudgetSummaryCard`) "perfectly mirrors the columns required by a professional permaculture phasing spreadsheet" — Phase × Season axis matches the OSU PDC Pro 5-year × 4-season template, and labor-hrs + cost-USD matches the official `$`/`Hrs` columns. OGDEN ships no phasing module. Verdict KEEP_ATLAS, no code change. Three enhancements logged as follow-ups: (1) optional `designLayer`/`scaleOfPermanence` enum on `PhaseTask` (Earthworks/Water/Vegetation/Structures) + matrix regrouping by Yeomans Keyline category; (2) capacity-validation against Client Survey baselines (weekly hrs, annual budget); (3) cumulative investment rollups (Yearly Running Total + 5-Year Total).
- [2026-05-07 Atlas Plan · Module 6 (Cross-section) — KEEP_ATLAS](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-plan-cross-section-scholar-keep-atlas.md) — Sixth module of the 8-step Permaculture Scholar adjudication. Scholar ruled Atlas's `TransectVerticalEditorCard` (540L: typed-ref pins + winter/summer solstice altitude lines) "the correct holistic framing" matching OSU PDC Assignment 15; OGDEN's swale-only section rejected. Verdict KEEP_ATLAS, no code change. Four enhancements logged as follow-ups: microclimate bracket labels, succession-stage bands, slope-% annotations, sector-response (wind/flow deflection) callouts.
- [2026-05-07 Atlas Plan · Module 5 (Soil Fertility) — BUILD_FRESH (additive)](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-plan-soil-scholar-build-fresh.md) — Fifth module of the 8-step Permaculture Scholar adjudication. Scholar ruled the 4-node fertility taxonomy too narrow, the WasteVectorTool "conceptually sound but useless without graphical validation," and demanded a baseline diagnosis before any amendment. Verdict BUILD_FRESH, additive. New `SoilBaselineCard` (jar test + percolation + pH → USDA 12-class texture-triangle SVG classifier + auto-derived limiting factors with permaculture remedies); new `ClosedLoopGraphCard` (ring-layout SVG of features + waste-vectors with orphan-fertility / no-feedstock / isolated-feature validations enforcing Holmgren P6 Produce No Waste). Atlas's two legacy cards retained as data-entry layer. Persistence, resource-inventory tab, and chronological soil-building plan deferred.
- [2026-05-07 Atlas Plan · Module 1 (Layering) — BUILD_FRESH (additive)](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-plan-layering-scholar-build-fresh.md) — Fourth module of the 8-step Permaculture Scholar adjudication. Scholar ruled Atlas's 9-rank Yeomans rollup orthodox but missing a spatial/relational view; OGDEN's collapsed 5-level scale violates Keyline (Access + Structures must remain distinct). Verdict BUILD_FRESH, additive. New `PermanenceLadderCard` reuses the 9 Zustand stores from the legacy `PermanenceScalesCard`, adds proportional bars + an Ordering check that walks per-rank prerequisites and warns when lower-permanence elements are placed before higher-permanence prerequisites are populated. Wired as second sub-tab `plan-permanence-ladder`; original tab kept.
- [2026-05-07 Atlas Plan · Module 3 (Zones & Circulation) — BUILD_FRESH (additive)](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-plan-zones-scholar-build-fresh.md) — Third module of the 8-step Permaculture Scholar adjudication. Scholar ruled the Atlas Z0–Z5 ladder *permaculturally orthodox* (Mollison) and rejected OGDEN's land-use categories + paddock-rotation page (the latter is properly Yeomans step 5, Subdivision, deferred to a future Subdivision/Livestock module). What was missing from Atlas: spatial visualisation. New `ZoneCirculationOverviewCard` projects existing zoneStore polygons + pathStore lines into an SVG mini-map with Z-coloured polygons + frequency-scaled path widths + bbox-overlap validation that flags daily/weekly paths not entering any Z1/Z2 zone. Atlas's `ZoneLevelLayer` and `PathFrequencyEditor` retained verbatim as the data-entry layer. OGDEN's movement-frequency heatmap excluded — depends on sensor data Atlas doesn't have.
- [2026-05-07 Atlas Plan · Module 2 (Water) — BUILD_FRESH per Scholar verdict](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-plan-water-scholar-build-fresh.md) — Second module of the 8-step Permaculture Scholar adjudication. Verdict BUILD_FRESH: Atlas current too abstract/non-spatial, OGDEN over-engineered (RUSLE/Q10). Architectural insight: directed graph of water nodes (Roofs → Tanks → Swales → Ponds) where every non-sink node MUST declare an overflow target (Mollison ch.7; Holmgren P2). Scope (b) scaled v1 — defer map-draw + topographic raster to follow-ups. New `WaterNode` type + `waterNodes` collection in `waterSystemsStore` (persist v2 → v3 migration). Three new cards under `apps/web/src/v3/plan/cards/water-management/`: catchments (V = A × P × C), storage/swale/sink with mandatory overflow target picker, and an SVG flow-graph + balance + orphan/cycle validation panel.
- [2026-05-07 Atlas Plan · Module 4 (Plants) — BUILD_FRESH per Scholar verdict](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-plan-plants-scholar-build-fresh.md) — First module of the 8-step Permaculture Scholar (NotebookLM `5aa3dcf3-…`) adjudication of Plan-stage modules. Verdict BUILD_FRESH (neither Atlas nor OGDEN sufficient). Three new cards under `apps/web/src/v3/plan/cards/plant-systems/`: site-match scoring on the Plant Database (hardiness-band overlap against `project.country`), spatial guild centroid placement on a parcel diagram with a water-flow arrow (centroid encoded into `Guild.notes` as `centroidUv:u,v` until schema gets a first-class field), and a six-layer (incl. root zone) cross-section across discrete scenarios Year 1/5/10/20/30+ with per-layer light attenuation. Atlas legacy `features/plan/Plant*Card.tsx` retained — still imported by `V3PlanPage.tsx` + `DashboardRouter.tsx`; consolidation deferred. Anchored in Mollison ch.10, OSU PDC *Tree Influence on Watershed*, and Holmgren P8.

- [2026-05-07 Atlas OBSERVE Lucide Point Symbology + Project-Scope GeoJSON / KML / CSV Export](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-observe-symbology-export.md) — Closes two more deferred items. NEW `lucideSprite.ts` registers eight MapLibre images (`observe-{neighbourPin,household,highPoint,soilSample}` plus four SWOT bucket variants) by rendering Lucide React icons via `renderToStaticMarkup`, wrapping in a 40×40 SVG with circular backdrop, decoding via `Image.decode()`, and calling `map.addImage(id, img, { pixelRatio: 2 })`; idempotent and re-runs on every `style.load`, with a `'styleimagemissing'` listener as backfill. Four `circle` layers in `ObserveAnnotationLayers` swap to `symbol`; mixed-kind layers use `['concat', 'observe-', ['get', 'annoKind' \| 'bucket']]` so a single layer dispatches per-feature icons. Selection halo unaffected (filter is geometry-type-keyed). NEW pure `annotationExport.ts` covers all 17 ExportKinds across the seven stores: `collectProjectAnnotations(projectId)` → `{ byKind, totalCount }`; `toGeoJSON(p)` (RFC 7946 FeatureCollection, geometry-less kinds skipped); `toKML(p)` (KML 2.2 hand-rolled XML, `<Folder>` per kind); `toCSV(p)` (multi-section, `# kind:` separators, union-of-columns headers, trailing `geometryWkt` WKT column — geometry-less records appear here only). Per-kind geometry resolver handles field heterogeneity (`position` / `location` / `center` / `pointA+pointB` / `geometry`). NEW `ExportButton.tsx` bottom-right floater + 3-format popover; Blob + anchor download; mounted from `ObserveLayout` next to `SelectionFloater`. 6 vitest specs pass; tsc + Vite build clean (34.62s). **Updated 2026-05-07:** sectors now round-trip into GeoJSON / KML when a homestead or parcel-boundary anchor exists (wedge polygon synthesised via the renderer's `wedgePolygon` math); the wedge outer radius is configurable per project via `metadata.sectorRadiusM` (NEW `sectorRadius.ts` helper, NEW numeric input in the Sectors / Zones slide-up, 250 m fallback for unset projects); `permacultureZone` now expands into six concentric Polygon Features in GeoJSON / six Placemarks in KML / one `MULTIPOLYGON` WKT row in CSV via a widened `geometriesFor` returning `KindGeom[]`, and `ecologyObservation` gains an optional `location?: [lng, lat]` field (Point in GeoJSON / KML when set, CSV-only otherwise); 16 / 16 specs pass
- [2026-05-07 Atlas OBSERVE Touch-First Drag + Multi-Item Batch Edit + Per-Store Undo Specs](decisions/2026-05-07-atlas-observe-batch-edit-touch-drag.md) — Closes the three deferred items from the 2026-05-06 selection/drag/zundo ADR. `AnnotationDragHandler` refactored from mouse-only into pointer-agnostic (`onLayerPointerDown`/`onPointerMove`/`onPointerUp`), wires both `mousedown`+`touchstart` on each point layer and `mouse{move,up}`+`touch{move,end}` on the global map; touch events gate on `e.originalEvent.touches.length === 1` so pinch-zoom never engages drag; a 4-pixel screen-space movement threshold prevents tap-to-select from being hijacked, and `map.touchZoomRotate.disableRotation()` is suspended only while the drag is engaged. `annotationFormStore.Active` widens to `mode: 'create' | 'edit' | 'edit-batch'` with `existingIds?: string[]`; `AnnotationFormSlideUp` seeds values from the first id and loops `schema.save()` once per id on Save (eyebrow reads `Edit ${n} ${kind}s`); `SelectionFloater` Edit gate widens to enable on same-kind multi-select (`selected.every((s) => s.kind === first.kind)`) with a tooltip explaining mixed-kind disablement. `temporal-undo.test.ts` extended with four new `describe` blocks (topography / externalForces / waterSystems / ecology) for 14 tests total — all seven OBSERVE namespace stores now have at least one `add → undo` and one `add+update → undo` spec passing under happy-dom. v1 batch undo is N-step (one zundo entry per patched record); `temporal.pause()`/`resume()` framing for single-step batch undo deferred. Tsc + Vite build clean (29.37s)
- [2026-05-06 Atlas OBSERVE Selection Floater + Drag-Reposition + Vertex Edit + zundo Global Undo](decisions/2026-05-06-atlas-observe-selection-drag-undo.md) — Closes the four items deferred from the same-day Edit/Delete ADR. `SelectionFloater` pill-bar (Edit/Delete/Clear + Esc) above the bottom rail; `AnnotationDragHandler` runs a live preview source while dragging a point and commits via `writePointPosition` from the new `annotationGeometryRegistry` (centralises kind→store-action routing because most points use `position` but soilSample uses nullable `location`); `AnnotationVertexEditHandler` spins up a dedicated headless MapboxDraw in `direct_select` mode for line/polygon vertex editing, gated against `useMapToolStore.activeTool` to avoid two-MapboxDraw collisions; zundo `temporal({ limit: 200 })` wraps each of the seven OBSERVE namespace stores _inside_ `persist()` so the undo timeline is in-memory only; `undoCoordinatorStore` keeps a global `history`/`redoHistory` of `UndoableStoreName` and dispatches `temporal.undo()`/`temporal.redo()` on the most-recently-mutated store, distinguishing forward mutations from coordinator-driven redo via an `inFlight` flag set during dispatch; `useGlobalAnnotationUndo` binds `Cmd/Ctrl-Z` (and -Y on Windows) on `document` with an INPUT/TEXTAREA/SELECT/contentEditable focus guard. Tsc + Vite build clean; 4 new vitest specs pass on humanContext / swot / soilSample (representative coverage of the uniform `persist(temporal(...))` pattern across all seven stores)

- [2026-04-30 Archive-v3 Blob Cleanup](decisions/2026-04-30-archive-v3-blob-cleanup.md) — Closes the final deferred item from the namespace ADR; new `cleanupArchivedV3()` export removes `ogden-site-annotations.archived-v3` on every boot after `migrateLegacyBlob()`; idempotent + vitest-covered (5 new specs); rollback hatch closed in favour of git-revert path
- [2026-04-30 TransectVerticalRef Resolver](decisions/2026-04-30-transect-vertical-ref-resolver.md) — Closes the deferred non-standalone-kind resolution from the namespace ADR; `TransectVerticalEditorCard` now resolves `water-system | polyculture | closed-loop | structure` refs against their domain stores at render time + adds a "Link to existing element" mode to the add-form; species heights via `PLANT_DATABASE.matureHeightM`, water-system/closed-loop heights via type-default lookups; missing refs render as soft warnings (amber `⚠`)
- [2026-04-30 uiStore stage3 Grouping Migration](decisions/2026-04-30-uistore-stage3-grouping-migration.md) — Returning users' persisted `sidebarGrouping: 'stage' | 'phase' | 'domain'` (carried over from before the 2026-04-29 default flip) hid the new ACT stage header in `DashboardSidebar`; bumps `uiStore` persist `version` 1→2 with a one-shot `migrate` that coerces stale values to `'stage3'`; idempotent (only `fromVersion < 2`); 7 vitest specs green; secondary: `rehydrate()` now guarded on `typeof window`
- [2026-04-30 Site-Annotations Store — Scholar-aligned 7-Namespace Consolidation](decisions/2026-04-30-site-annotations-store-scholar-aligned-namespaces.md) — Decompose the 13-family `siteAnnotationsStore` v3 god-store into 7 Scholar-aligned namespace Zustand stores (`externalForcesStore` hazards+sectors / `topographyStore` transects / `ecologyStore` ecology+succession / `waterSystemsStore` earthworks+storageInfra / `polycultureStore` guilds+species / `closedLoopStore` wasteVectors+runs+fertilityInfra / `swotStore` swot); `Transect.verticalElements` → `Transect.verticalRefs: TransectVerticalRef[]` discriminated union (standalone | water-system | polyculture | closed-loop | structure); idempotent `migrateLegacyBlob()` at boot archives v3 as `ogden-site-annotations.archived-v3`; type-only `site-annotations.ts` barrel + relocated `newAnnotationId`; 24 consumer files swap imports; supersedes 2026-04-29 13-per-family proposal
- [2026-04-30 V3 DesignPage Live Canvas — Scoping](decisions/2026-04-30-v3-design-canvas-scoping.md) — *(proposed)* Phase 5.1 scoping ADR: build `DesignMap.tsx` mirroring `DiagnoseMap` (no MapboxDraw runtime); reuse v2 zone/structure/path/livestock/crop stores rather than a v3 shadow store; deterministic single-pass snap (boundary edge → structure corner → path centerline) at 8 px screen radius; live `computeAssessmentScores` recompute throttled to 250 ms via `requestIdleCallback` keyed off `(count, lastMutationMs)` per store; new `DesignScoreCallout` strip surfaces score-delta vs. pre-design baseline; ~1,200 LOC across 4 sequenced PRs; defers drag-edit/vertex-edit, multi-select, score-aware undo
- [2026-04-30 V3 OperatePage Field Map — Scoping](decisions/2026-04-30-v3-operate-field-map-scoping.md) — *(proposed)* Phase 5.2 scoping ADR: build `OperateMap.tsx` mirroring `DiagnoseMap`; promote `FieldFlag.x/y` (0–100 pseudo-coords) to `position: [lng, lat]` + add `source` and `observedAt`; `useFieldFlags(projectId)` derives flags from `useLivestockStore` paddocks + `useWaterSystemsStore` storage + weather alerts, unioned with brief fallbacks for `fence`/`team` until those stores ship; single MapLibre symbol layer with kind-driven icons + tone-driven `icon-color`; 60 s `visibilityState`-gated polling for sensor-driven flags; "Log Observation" wires today, "Create Field Task" waits on Phase 6.4; ~830 LOC across 4 PRs
- [2026-04-30 V3 DiagnosePage Parcel Satellite Snapshot](decisions/2026-04-30-v3-parcel-satellite-snapshot.md) — Phase 5.3 closure: replaces the `◊` glyph in the DiagnosePage StageHero aside with a server-rendered MapTiler satellite tile + SVG-polygon boundary outline; web-mercator forward projection picks zoom from the parcel bbox; falls back to the prior glyph card when no MapTiler key is configured or the project has no boundary polygon; pure visual surface (no stores, no maplibregl runtime); 5.1 (Design canvas) + 5.2 (Operate field map) remain ADR-gated as larger scope
- [2026-04-30 V3 Score Adapter — 8→6 Mapping](decisions/2026-04-30-v3-score-adapter-8-to-6-mapping.md) — Phase 4.2 reconciliation: shared scorer's 8 weighted labels collapse into v3's 6 plain-language `ProjectScores` categories (`landFit ← avg(Ag Suitability, Regen Potential, Stewardship Readiness)` / `water ← Water Resilience` / `regulation ← Habitat Sensitivity` / `access ← Buildability` / `financial ← Community Suitability` / `designCompleteness ← 100 − Design Complexity`); weakest-wins confidence rollup; 6-tier verdict threshold table on `computeOverallScore`; new `adaptLocalProject.ts` + `adaptScores.ts` adapter pair; `useV3Project` keyed on `(projectId, projects, dataByProject)` so v3 pages re-render when layer fetches complete; placeholder fallback when `siteData.status !== 'complete'` so v3 renders honest empty state; Regulation/Financial proxies move 1:1 when dedicated scorers ship in Phase 7
- [2026-05-15 Atlas Spec Reconciliation + MVP Delta](decisions/2026-05-15-atlas-spec-reconciliation-mvp-delta.md) — Reconciles OGDEN's `OLOS_Atlas_Platform_Workflow_Spec_v1` against the codebase (more mature than its "prototype" assumption); six scoped v3-only workstreams: spec-taxonomy mapping (WS2), regeneration methodology content (WS4), Barren/Compacted system obligation woven at `runAutoDesign` not `sequencingEngine` (WS3), editable boundary → API sync gated on real boundary change (WS1), server-side `capital_partner_summary` PDF (WS5 Part 1), soft non-blocking `ObserveReadyCue` (WS6); answers spec OQ1–OQ5; WS5 Part 2 (tokenized public share route) + WS4b (maintenance rollup) deferred; tsc clean, 77 tests green
- [2026-05-15 WS5 P2 Public Report Share + WS4b Maintenance Rollup](decisions/2026-05-15-atlas-ws5p2-public-report-share-ws4b-maintenance.md) — Closes the two deferred MVP-delta items. WS5 P2: tokenized unauthenticated view-only report share reusing `project_portals` (no migration), `config.reportShare` with its own publish flag; public route **streams the frozen `capital_partner_summary` PDF bytes through the API** so the raw storage URL is never client-visible (resolves the storage-ACL security checkpoint by design), `Cache-Control: no-store` for immediate unpublish. WS4b: pure `computeMaintenanceSchedule` → synthetic recurring phase (order 99) + `isMaintenanceTask` tasks woven at the `runAutoDesign` seam (mirrors `regenerationForcing`), `MaintenanceSchedule` metadata on 19 interventions + 2 regen methods, new `MaintenanceScheduleCard`. Fixes a latent `GenerateSiteDesignBar` bug that silently dropped WS3+WS4b synthetic-phase tasks (`AutoDesignResult.generatedPhases` now combined). tsc clean; web 158/158, api portal 8/8 green
- [2026-05-15 Regenerative Farm Catalog — First-Class Cash Enterprises](decisions/2026-05-15-atlas-regenerative-farm-catalog-cash-enterprises.md) — Closes OQ1 for the Regenerative Farm archetype (was partial: no market-scale horticulture / broadacre rotation). Adds `market-garden` (commercial Zone-2 beds, distinct from subsistence `kitchen-garden`) + `annual-cash-crop-rotation` (regenerative broadacre, dominant field share) to `interventionCatalog.ts` — authored to the existing schema + selectable by the existing `income-*`/`soil-*` criterion vocabulary, **no engine/schema/criterion change** (gap was content, not vocabulary). Both carry WS4b maintenance metadata. tsc clean; `src/v3/plan` 84/84 (4 new `regenerativeFarmCatalog.test.ts`). Retreat Center / Educational Farm / Conservation / Multi-Enterprise stay OQ1-blocked pending the project-type-list decision
- [2026-05-15 Satellite Basemap → Esri World Imagery](decisions/2026-05-15-atlas-satellite-basemap-esri-world-imagery.md) — `satellite` basemap swapped from MapTiler to a free/no-token inline Esri World Imagery raster style (`ESRI_WORLD_IMAGERY_STYLE` in `maplibre.ts`, ~z19, MapTiler `glyphs` fallback for label layers); `MAP_STYLES` type widened to `string | StyleSpecification`; MapTiler satellite retained (and as fallback) via the **Hybrid** style; no zoom/fit/precache/store-default change. Typecheck clean across all 9 consumers; live `getStyle()` + round-trip + Hybrid-fallback verified, no Esri/CORS/glyph errors
- [2026-05-15 Offline Tile-Precache Esri Parity](decisions/2026-05-15-atlas-offline-tile-precache-esri-parity.md) — Follow-up to the basemap swap: offline cache now matches the live Satellite source. New Workbox `StaleWhileRevalidate` rule for `server.arcgisonline.com/.../World_Imagery/*` into the **same** `ogden-map-tiles` bucket (serves both the live raster fetches and the precache warmer — the essential fix; MapTiler rules untouched); `tilePrecache.ts` repointed `MAPTILER_TILE_BASE`→`ESRI_TILE_BASE`, `buildTileUrl` → `tile/{z}/{y}/{x}` (no @2x/.jpg/key), `VITE_MAPTILER_KEY` gate removed so keyless public deploy gains offline satellite; `MAX_TILES`/zoom-range/concurrency unchanged. tsc + build exit 0, `dist/sw.js` carries the Esri route + shared bucket ×2, 2 new `tilePrecache.test.ts` specs green; behavioural offline DevTools step deferred (renderer-hang env)
- [2026-05-15 Plan Map-View IA — ModuleBar in slide-up + Vision-first order](decisions/2026-05-15-atlas-plan-modulebar-in-slideup-and-view-order.md) — Optional `topBar?: ReactNode` slot on the shared `ModuleSlideUp` (first sheet child, above `<header>`, new `.topBar` wrapper); `PlanLayout` feeds the **same stateless `PlanModuleBar` element** into both `StageShell.bottomTray` (closed, unchanged) and the slide-up `topBar` (open) so the module navigator stays reachable while a module page is open — open/close + switch semantics unchanged. Additive/backward-compatible (Act/Observe omit `topBar`). Also: `PLAN_VIEWS` reordered `['vision','current','terrain3d']` + `PlanLayout` default view `'current'→'vision'`. Preview-verified; pre-existing `mtc` fallback redirect (resets slide-up state) left as-is
- [2026-05-16 Atlas Catalog Archetype Parity (closes OQ1)](decisions/2026-05-16-atlas-catalog-archetype-parity.md) — Closes spec OQ1 for **all six** archetypes (catalog depth was the last open WS4 item). New `ProjectArchetype` named union + optional `Intervention.projectTypes?` tag; sequencing-engine eligibility loop skips an intervention whose non-empty `projectTypes` excludes the active archetype (untagged ⇒ universal ⇒ 22 legacy entries provably non-regressive). `interventionCatalog.ts` split into `interventionCatalog/` (`_shared` 22 verbatim + per-archetype modules + barrel `index`); original path kept as thin re-export ⇒ zero importer churn. 24 new grounded interventions (6 per non-homestead archetype) + shared cross-vocab `criterionContributions` on ~13 legacy entries; `CATALOG_VERSION → goal-compass-v2-2026-05-16`. New `archetypeCatalogParity.test.ts` 15/15 (≥6 distinct selected per archetype + grounded + id-uniqueness + foundations untagged); legacy regen test unchanged & green; plan-engine 102/102; tsc clean. `multi-largest-enterprise-pct` left without a dedicated contribution (emergent ratio)
- [2026-05-16 Selection Floaters Share One Stacking Container](decisions/2026-05-16-atlas-selection-floater-stacking.md) — Overlapping zone + adopted-building selections rendered Observe `SelectionFloater` and `PlanSelectionFloater` pills at identical `absolute` bottom-center coords (lower bar's actions unreachable). Both now `createPortal` into a body-level singleton `<div data-floater-stack>` (`floaterStackRoot.ts`); positioning moved off `.floater` onto a `.stack` flex column (`gap:8px`, `pointer-events:none`, re-anchors above `[data-stage-bottom]`, CSS `bottom:16px` fallback); stable inline `order` (Observe 1 upper / Plan 2 lower). No selection/click/layout-mount change; only the 2 `.tsx` import that CSS module. tsc clean; geometric `getBoundingClientRect` proof of stacking/gap/centering
- [2026-05-16 Feature-Edit Popover Fixed Right-Edge Dock](decisions/2026-05-16-atlas-inline-popover-fixed-dock.md) — Steward-reported: the shared `InlineFeaturePopover` (Plan/Observe/Act) was clipped behind the module bar for bottom-edge features. Dropped feature-`[lng,lat]` anchoring + the `map.project()` re-projection `useEffect` + the horizontal auto-flip; `.popover` now a fixed dock (`absolute; top:56px; right:12px; z-index:6; max-height:calc(100% - 56px - 96px); overflow-y:auto`) clearing the `DesignToolRail` and bottom bar, long forms scroll inside. `map` prop retained as `_props` (zero call-site churn). Companion: `StageShell` now tags its bottom tray `data-stage-bottom` (the attribute the prior floater-stacking fix assumed pre-existing). tsc clean; live stylesheet + `getBoundingClientRect` proof; screenshot/cross-stage pass deferred (canvas hangs capture, 0-size preview env)
- [2026-05-16 Act §5.2 Plan-Execution Tracker](decisions/2026-05-16-atlas-act-plan-execution-tracker.md) — Closes spec §5.2 (interactive task dashboard; MVP shipped only a navigable plan doc). Additive optional `PhaseTask.done?/doneAt?` + `toggleTaskDone(phaseId,taskId)` mirroring `overrideGoalCompassTask` but **not** setting `status:'overridden'` (no persist bump — `isMaintenanceTask?` precedent). New dedicated Act module `'tracker'` (ordered first; delegated UX call — `phaseStore` *is* the ledger, distinct from Schedule/Build); new `PlanExecutionTrackerCard` (raw-`phases` + `useMemo` derive per selector-stability rule, per-phase/overall %, overdue vs `scheduledStart`, designLayer pivot, maintenance badge, toast). Discovered + resolved a second source of truth: `ActModuleId` Zod enum in `@ogden/shared` (telemetry) is hand-synced with `ActModule` — both must gain a new module or tsc fails at `record()` sites; migration 024 CHECK is on `event_type` only so the `module` column is unconstrained ⇒ enum-extend is DB-safe. tsc clean; `src/store` 98/98 (new 6-spec toggle test); plan-engine 110/110; preview end-to-end (mark-done/reopen + progress + overdue + strikethrough + toast, localStorage persist version still 3, survives reload)
- [2026-05-18 ObserveModuleBar `<button>`-in-`<button>` nesting fix](decisions/2026-05-18-atlas-observe-modulebar-button-nesting.md) — Pre-existing React `validateDOMNesting` warning on the Observe stage (outer tile `<button>` wrapped inner per-task `subseg` `<button>`s). Outer element converted `<button>` → `<div role="button" tabIndex={0}>` with an Enter/Space `onKeyDown` (`preventDefault` so Space doesn't scroll) → `handleCardClick`; `aria-pressed`/`onClick`/`css.tile`/`css.tileActive` preserved (zero visual change), inner sub-seg buttons now legally nested and keep `stopPropagation`+navigate. Removed redundant outer `type="button"`. tsc clean for `ObserveModuleBar` (other run errors are worktree env artifacts — no installed `node_modules`); in-browser preview deferred (deps not installable in this isolated worktree)

## Design System
- [IA & Panel Conventions](../design-system/ogden-atlas/ia-and-panel-conventions.md) — Perimeter strategy, z-index scales, rail/popover/modal decision matrix, map-floating inventory; codifies UX Scholar audit §§1 + 3 (P2)
- [UX Scholar Audit](../design-system/ogden-atlas/ui-ux-scholar-audit.md) — Six-area UI/UX audit with P0/P1/P2 findings (source of the conventions spec and two 2026-04-23 ADRs)
